const CONFIG = {
  gap: 24,
  padding: 24,
  stroke: 4,
  radius: 16,
  baseHeight: 60,
  scaffoldStroke: 6,
};

// --- CORE STRUCTURAL COMPONENTS ---

const AnimatedToggle = ({ open, size = 32 }) => (
  <div
    className="relative group flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 cursor-pointer bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-[0px_0px_0px_0px_black] transition-all"
    style={{ width: size, height: size }}
  >
    {open ? (
      <Minimize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />
    ) : (
      <Maximize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />
    )}
  </div>
);

const MainToolbox = ({ title, icon: Icon, themeColor, children, defaultOpen = true }) => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(defaultOpen);

  return (
    <div
      className="w-full bg-white flex flex-col overflow-hidden relative shadow-[12px_12px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.8)] transition-all mb-12"
      style={{
        border: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black`,
        borderRadius: `${CONFIG.radius}px`,
      }}
    >
      <header
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
        className="h-[80px] min-h-[80px] flex items-center justify-between select-none z-30 relative cursor-pointer transition-[margin] duration-500"
        style={{
          backgroundColor: themeColor,
          borderBottom: isOpen ? `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` : "0px",
        }}
      >
        <div className="flex items-center h-full flex-1">
          <div
            className="h-full w-[80px] flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 bg-white"
            style={{ borderRight: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` }}
          >
            <Icon size={40} strokeWidth={2.5} className="text-black" />
          </div>
          <h2 className="text-[32px] sm:text-[40px] md:text-[50px] font-[1000] uppercase tracking-tighter leading-none pl-6 truncate text-black">
            {title}
          </h2>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 pr-6 h-full">
          <AnimatedToggle open={isOpen} size={44} />
        </div>
      </header>

      <div
        className={`grid transition-[grid-template-rows] duration-500 ease-[cubic-bezier(0.4,0,0.2,1)] ${
          isOpen ? "grid-rows-[1fr]" : "grid-rows-[0fr]"
        }`}
      >
        <div className="overflow-hidden min-h-0 bg-neutral-100 p-4 sm:p-6 lg:p-8 space-y-6">
          {children}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const SubToolbox = ({ title, icon: Icon, headerBg, iconBg, children }) => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(true);

  return (
    <div
      className="w-full bg-white overflow-hidden relative flex flex-col shrink-0 transition-all duration-300 shadow-[6px_6px_0px_0px_black]"
      style={{
        border: `${CONFIG.stroke}px solid black`,
        borderRadius: `${CONFIG.radius}px`,
      }}
    >
      <header
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
        className="flex items-center justify-between select-none relative z-20 cursor-pointer h-[56px] min-h-[56px]"
        style={{
          backgroundColor: headerBg,
          borderBottom: isOpen ? `${CONFIG.stroke}px solid black` : "0px",
        }}
      >
        <div className="flex items-center h-full flex-1">
          <div
            className="h-full w-[56px] flex items-center justify-center shrink-0"
            style={{
              backgroundColor: iconBg,
              borderRight: `${CONFIG.stroke}px solid black`,
            }}
          >
            <Icon size={28} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center pl-4 h-full pointer-events-none select-none">
            <h3 className="font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black leading-none text-[28px] mt-1">
              {title}
            </h3>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 pr-4 h-full">
          <AnimatedToggle open={isOpen} size={28} />
        </div>
      </header>

      <div
        className={`grid transition-[grid-template-rows] duration-500 ${
          isOpen ? "grid-rows-[1fr]" : "grid-rows-[0fr]"
        }`}
      >
        <div className="overflow-hidden min-h-0">
          <main className="bg-[#f3f4f6] w-full p-4 md:p-6 text-black flex flex-col gap-6">
            {children}
          </main>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const ComponentShowcase = ({ title, layout = "single", children }) => {
  const layoutClasses = {
    single: "grid-cols-1",
    pair: "grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2",
    grid: "grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-4",
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
      <div className="h-8 border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg bg-white px-3 inline-flex items-center self-start shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black]">
        <span className="text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">{title}</span>
      </div>
      <div className={`grid ${layoutClasses[layout]} gap-6 w-full`}>{children}</div>
    </div>
  );
};

const VariantLabel = ({ type }) => {
  const isCreative = type === "Creative";
  return (
    <div
      className={`absolute -top-3 -right-3 px-3 py-1 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest z-10 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] ${
        isCreative ? "bg-[#B28DFF] text-black" : "bg-[#FFE357] text-black"
      }`}
    >
      {type}
    </div>
  );
};

import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from "react";
import {
  Activity, BarChart3, Bell, Check, ChevronDown, ChevronUp, ChevronRight,
  Circle, Code, Eye, EyeOff, Filter, Layers, Layout, Maximize2, Minimize2,
  MonitorPlay, Play, Pause, Settings, ShieldAlert, SlidersHorizontal, Square,
  Terminal, ToggleRight, TrendingUp, X, Zap, AlertTriangle, CheckCircle2,
  Info, Loader2, Home, Users, Folder, Search, Image as ImageIcon, MessageSquare,
  Edit2, Trash2, MoreVertical, FastForward, Rewind, Volume2
} from "lucide-react";

// --- CONFIGURATION & UTILS ---
const CONFIG = {
  stroke: 4, radius: 16, scaffoldStroke: 6,
};

const COLORS = {
  yellow: "#FFE357", pink: "#FF7497", blue: "#24D3FF", lime: "#CCFF00",
  orange: "#FCAF57", purple: "#B28DFF", dark: "#1A1A24", white: "#FFFFFF",
};

// --- CORE STRUCTURAL COMPONENTS ---
const AnimatedToggle = ({ open, size = 32 }) => (
  <div
    className="relative flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 cursor-pointer bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-[0px_0px_0px_0px_black] transition-all"
    style={{ width: size, height: size }}
  >
    {open ? <Minimize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" /> : <Maximize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />}
  </div>
);

const MainToolbox = ({ title, icon: Icon, themeColor, children, defaultOpen = true }) => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(defaultOpen);
  return (
    <div className="w-full bg-white flex flex-col overflow-hidden relative shadow-[12px_12px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.8)] transition-all mb-12" style={{ border: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black`, borderRadius: `${CONFIG.radius}px` }}>
      <header onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)} className="h-[80px] min-h-[80px] flex items-center justify-between select-none z-30 relative cursor-pointer" style={{ backgroundColor: themeColor, borderBottom: isOpen ? `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` : "0px" }}>
        <div className="flex items-center h-full flex-1">
          <div className="h-full w-[80px] flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 bg-white" style={{ borderRight: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` }}>
            <Icon size={40} strokeWidth={2.5} className="text-black" />
          </div>
          <h2 className="text-[32px] sm:text-[40px] md:text-[50px] font-[1000] uppercase tracking-tighter leading-none pl-6 truncate text-black">{title}</h2>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center pr-6 h-full"><AnimatedToggle open={isOpen} size={44} /></div>
      </header>
      <div className={`grid transition-[grid-template-rows] duration-500 ease-in-out ${isOpen ? "grid-rows-[1fr]" : "grid-rows-[0fr]"}`}>
        <div className="overflow-hidden min-h-0 bg-neutral-100 p-4 sm:p-6 lg:p-8 space-y-6">{children}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const SubToolbox = ({ title, icon: Icon, headerBg, iconBg, children }) => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(true);
  return (
    <div className="w-full bg-white overflow-hidden relative flex flex-col shrink-0 transition-all duration-300 shadow-[6px_6px_0px_0px_black]" style={{ border: `${CONFIG.stroke}px solid black`, borderRadius: `${CONFIG.radius}px` }}>
      <header onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)} className="flex items-center justify-between select-none relative z-20 cursor-pointer h-[56px] min-h-[56px]" style={{ backgroundColor: headerBg, borderBottom: isOpen ? `${CONFIG.stroke}px solid black` : "0px" }}>
        <div className="flex items-center h-full flex-1">
          <div className="h-full w-[56px] flex items-center justify-center shrink-0" style={{ backgroundColor: iconBg, borderRight: `${CONFIG.stroke}px solid black` }}>
            <Icon size={28} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />
          </div>
          <h3 className="font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black leading-none text-[28px] mt-1 pl-4 pointer-events-none select-none">{title}</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center pr-4 h-full"><AnimatedToggle open={isOpen} size={28} /></div>
      </header>
      <div className={`grid transition-[grid-template-rows] duration-500 ${isOpen ? "grid-rows-[1fr]" : "grid-rows-[0fr]"}`}>
        <div className="overflow-hidden min-h-0"><main className="bg-[#f3f4f6] w-full p-4 md:p-6 text-black flex flex-col gap-6">{children}</main></div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const ComponentShowcase = ({ title, layout = "single", children }) => {
  const layoutClasses = { single: "grid-cols-1", pair: "grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2", grid: "grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-4" };
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
      <div className="h-8 border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg bg-white px-3 inline-flex items-center self-start shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black]">
        <span className="text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">{title}</span>
      </div>
      <div className={`grid ${layoutClasses[layout]} gap-6 w-full`}>{children}</div>
    </div>
  );
};

const VariantLabel = ({ type }) => (
  <div className={`absolute -top-3 -right-3 px-3 py-1 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest z-20 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] ${type === "Tokyo-Pop" ? "bg-[#B28DFF] text-black" : "bg-[#FFE357] text-black"}`}>
    {type}
  </div>
);

        <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={h1} onChange={(e)=>setH1(e.target.value)} className="w-full h-4 bg-[#f3f4f6] border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none outline-none overflow-hidden cursor-pointer" style={{boxShadow: "inset 0 0 0 1px black", background: `linear-gradient(to right, ${COLORS.lime} ${h1}%, #f3f4f6 ${h1}%)`}} />
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop Horizontal Range */}

        <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-[#24D3FF] mb-3"><span>SYS_OVERRIDE</span><span className="text-[#CCFF00]">{h2}</span></div>
        <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={h2} onChange={(e)=>setH2(e.target.value)} className="w-full h-2 bg-black border-[2px] border-[#FF7497] rounded-none appearance-none outline-none cursor-pointer" style={{background: `linear-gradient(to right, ${COLORS.blue} ${h2}%, black ${h2}%)`}} />
        <div className="flex justify-between mt-2 px-1">{[...Array(10)].map((_,i) => <div key={i} className="w-[2px] h-2 bg-[#B28DFF] opacity-50"/>)}</div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Standard Vertical */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-56 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">

          <div className="w-full bg-[#FF7497] border-t-[3px] border-black transition-all" style={{height: `${v1}%`}} />
          <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={v1} onChange={(e)=>setV1(e.target.value)} className="absolute inset-0 w-32 h-4 -translate-x-[56px] translate-y-[56px] -rotate-90 appearance-none bg-transparent outline-none cursor-pointer" />
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop Vertical */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-56 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#FF7497]">
         <div className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-[#FF7497] mb-4 w-full text-center">LVL_{v2}</div>
         <div className="relative h-32 w-8 bg-black border-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] flex flex-col-reverse items-center justify-start p-1 gap-1">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#CCFF00] opacity-20 transition-all origin-bottom" style={{transform: `scaleY(${v2/100})`}}/>
            {[...Array(10)].map((_,i) => <div key={i} className={`w-full h-2 ${i < v2/10 ? 'bg-[#CCFF00] shadow-[0_0_8px_#CCFF00]' : 'bg-[#1A1A24] border border-[#24D3FF]/30'} transition-all`} />)}
            <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={v2} onChange={(e)=>setV2(e.target.value)} className="absolute inset-0 w-32 h-8 -translate-x-[48px] translate-y-[48px] -rotate-90 appearance-none bg-transparent outline-none cursor-pointer opacity-0" />

  return (

const HeatgridPack = () => {
  const generateGrid = (rows, cols, isCreative) => {
    let cells = [];
    const colors = isCreative ? ["#1A1A24", "#FF7497", "#B28DFF", "#24D3FF", "#CCFF00"] : ["#ffffff", "#f3f4f6", "#FFE357", "#FCAF57", "#FF7497"];
    for(let r=0; r<rows; r++) {
      for(let c=0; c<cols; c++) {
        const val = Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length);
        cells.push(<div key={`${r}-${c}`} className={`w-full aspect-square border-[2px] border-black rounded-sm shadow-[1px_1px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: colors[val]}} />);
      }
    }
    return cells;
  };

  return (
    <ComponentShowcase title="Data Map: Heatgrids" layout="pair">
      {/* Standard Heatgrid */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col gap-3 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">
        <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
        <div className="text-[11px] font-black uppercase">Activity Map</div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 w-full">{generateGrid(5, 12, false)}</div>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[8px] font-black uppercase mt-1 opacity-60"><span>Jan</span><span>Dec</span></div>
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop Heatgrid */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col gap-3 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#FF7497]">
        <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
        <div className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-[#FF7497]">NODE_DENSITY</div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 w-full">{generateGrid(5, 12, true)}</div>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[8px] font-black uppercase mt-1 text-[#24D3FF] tracking-widest"><span>T-MINUS</span><span>T-ZERO</span></div>
      </div>
    </ComponentShowcase>
  );
};

const ResearchTablePack = () => {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState({ 1: true });
  const [sortOrder, setSortOrder] = useState('desc');

  const data = [
    { id: 1, name: "UX Study Alpha", status: "Active", score: 94, sub: "Tested 40 users. Heatmap shows 80% scroll depth." },
    { id: 2, name: "Beta Conversion", status: "Paused", score: 62, sub: "Requires UI refresh. CTR dropped 15%." },
    { id: 3, name: "Omega Testing", status: "Active", score: 88, sub: "Validating new Neo-Brutal components." },
  ];

  const sortedData = [...data].sort((a,b) => sortOrder === 'desc' ? b.score - a.score : a.score - b.score);

  return (
    <ComponentShowcase title="Complex Research Table" layout="single">
      {/* Standard Table */}
      <div className="border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] overflow-hidden mb-6">

          <div className="col-span-5">Project Name</div>
          <div className="col-span-3">Status</div>
          <div className="col-span-3 flex items-center gap-1 cursor-pointer hover:bg-black/10 p-1 rounded-md" onClick={()=>setSortOrder(sortOrder==='desc'?'asc':'desc')}>
            Score {sortOrder === 'desc' ? <ChevronDown size={14}/> : <ChevronUp size={14}/>}
          </div>
        </div>
        {/* Body */}
        <div className="divide-y-[3px] divide-black">
          {sortedData.map((row) => (
            <React.Fragment key={row.id}>
              {/* Main Row */}
              <div className="bg-white p-3 grid grid-cols-12 items-center gap-2 text-[12px] font-bold hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors">
                <div className="col-span-1 flex justify-center cursor-pointer" onClick={()=>setExpanded({...expanded, [row.id]: !expanded[row.id]})}>
                  {expanded[row.id] ? <ChevronDown size={18}/> : <ChevronRight size={18}/>}
                </div>
                <div className="col-span-5 truncate">{row.name}</div>
                <div className="col-span-3 flex items-center gap-2">
                  <div className={`w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black rounded-full ${row.status === 'Active' ? 'bg-[#CCFF00]' : 'bg-[#FF7497]'}`} />
                  <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-black">{row.status}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="col-span-3 flex items-center justify-between">
                  <span className="font-black text-lg leading-none">{row.score}</span>
                  <div className="flex gap-1">
                    <button className="w-8 h-8 bg-[#24D3FF] border-[2px] border-black rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-none"><Edit2 size={12}/></button>
                    <button className="w-8 h-8 bg-[#FF7497] border-[2px] border-black rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-none"><Trash2 size={12}/></button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* Nested Row */}
              {expanded[row.id] && (
                <div className="bg-[#f3f4f6] p-4 border-t-[2px] border-dashed border-black/30">
                  <div className="ml-8 border-[3px] border-black bg-white p-3 rounded-xl shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black]">
                    <span className="text-[9px] font-black uppercase text-black/50 block mb-1">Details_Log</span>

                    <button className="mt-3 px-3 py-1 bg-black text-white text-[9px] font-black uppercase rounded-md shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_#CCFF00]">View Full Report</button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

// Helpers for NavigationPack
const ChevronLeftIcon = () => <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="3" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"><path d="m15 18-6-6 6-6"/></svg>;
const ChevronRightIcon = () => <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="3" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"><path d="m9 18 6-6-6-6"/></svg>;

// --- 6. COMPLEXITY PACK (OTP, Color Picker, Video Player) ---

const OTPPack = () => {
  const [code1, setCode1] = useState(Array(6).fill(''));
  const [code2, setCode2] = useState(Array(6).fill(''));
  const inputs1 = useRef([]);
  const inputs2 = useRef([]);

  const handleChange = (e, index, isCreative) => {
    const val = e.target.value.slice(-1);
    if(isCreative) {
      const newCode = [...code2]; newCode[index] = val; setCode2(newCode);
      if(val && index < 5) inputs2.current[index+1].focus();
    } else {
      const newCode = [...code1]; newCode[index] = val; setCode1(newCode);
      if(val && index < 5) inputs1.current[index+1].focus();
    }
  };

  return (
    <ComponentShowcase title="6-Digit OTP Inputs" layout="pair">
      {/* Standard OTP */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col justify-center items-center h-48 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">
        <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
        <span className="text-[12px] font-black uppercase mb-4">Enter Auth Code</span>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          {code1.map((num, i) => (
            <input key={i} ref={el => inputs1.current[i] = el} type="text" value={num} onChange={(e)=>handleChange(e,i,false)} className="w-10 h-14 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#f3f4f6] text-center text-xl font-black shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black] focus:bg-[#FFE357] focus:outline-none transition-colors" />
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop OTP */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col justify-center items-center h-48 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#FF7497]">
        <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
        <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-[#FF7497] mb-4">DECRYPTION_KEY</span>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          {code2.map((num, i) => (
            <input key={i} ref={el => inputs2.current[i] = el} type="text" value={num} onChange={(e)=>handleChange(e,i,true)} className="w-10 h-14 border-[2px] border-transparent border-b-[#24D3FF] bg-black text-center text-xl font-mono text-[#CCFF00] shadow-[0_4px_0_0_rgba(36,211,255,0.2)] focus:border-[#CCFF00] focus:shadow-[0_4px_0_0_#CCFF00] focus:outline-none transition-all" />
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </ComponentShowcase>
  );
};

const ColorPickerPack = () => {
  const [activeColor1, setActiveColor1] = useState(COLORS.lime);
  const [activeColor2, setActiveColor2] = useState(COLORS.pink);
  
  const stdColors = [COLORS.lime, COLORS.pink, COLORS.blue, COLORS.yellow, COLORS.orange, "#ffffff", "#000000", "#9ca3af"];
  const tpColors = ["#CCFF00", "#FF7497", "#24D3FF", "#B28DFF", "#FF0055", "#00FF9D", "#7000FF", "#1A1A24"];

  return (
    <ComponentShowcase title="Color Swatch Pickers" layout="pair">
      {/* Standard Swatch */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col justify-between h-56 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">
        <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
        <div className="flex gap-4">
          <div className="w-16 h-16 border-[4px] border-black rounded-2xl shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] transition-colors" style={{backgroundColor: activeColor1}}/>
          <div className="flex flex-col justify-center">
             <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase">Selected Hex</span>
             <span className="text-xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter">{activeColor1}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mt-4">
          {stdColors.map(c => (
            <button key={c} onClick={()=>setActiveColor1(c)} className={`w-full aspect-square border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg transition-transform ${activeColor1===c ? 'scale-110 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] z-10' : 'hover:scale-105'}`} style={{backgroundColor: c}}/>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop Swatch */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col justify-between h-56 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#CCFF00]">
        <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
        <div className="flex gap-4 items-center border-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] p-2 bg-black">
          <div className="w-10 h-10 border-[2px] border-black shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(255,255,255,0.2)] transition-colors" style={{backgroundColor: activeColor2, boxShadow: `0 0 15px ${activeColor2}`}}/>
          <span className="text-lg font-mono text-white tracking-widest">{activeColor2}</span>
        </div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mt-4">
          {tpColors.map(c => (
            <button key={c} onClick={()=>setActiveColor2(c)} className={`w-full h-8 border-[2px] border-black transition-all ${activeColor2===c ? 'shadow-[0_0_10px_white] scale-105 z-10' : 'opacity-60 hover:opacity-100'}`} style={{backgroundColor: c}}/>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </ComponentShowcase>
  );
};

import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from "react";
import {
  Activity, BarChart3, Bell, Check, ChevronDown, ChevronUp, ChevronRight,
  Circle, Code, Eye, EyeOff, Filter, Layers, Layout, Maximize2, Minimize2,
  MonitorPlay, Play, Pause, Settings, ShieldAlert, SlidersHorizontal, Square,
  Terminal, ToggleRight, TrendingUp, X, Zap, AlertTriangle, CheckCircle2,
  Info, Loader2, Home, Users, Folder, Search, Image as ImageIcon, MessageSquare,
  Edit2, Trash2, MoreVertical, FastForward, Rewind, Volume2,
  Star, Calendar as CalendarIcon, UploadCloud, User, CreditCard, Tag, PieChart,
  TrendingDown, ArrowUpRight, ArrowDownRight, Compass, Shield, Database, Cpu, Plus
} from "lucide-react";

// --- CONFIGURATION & UTILS ---
const CONFIG = {
  stroke: 4, radius: 16, scaffoldStroke: 6,
};

const COLORS = {
  yellow: "#FFE357", pink: "#FF7497", blue: "#24D3FF", lime: "#CCFF00",
  orange: "#FCAF57", purple: "#B28DFF", dark: "#1A1A24", white: "#FFFFFF",
};

// --- CORE STRUCTURAL COMPONENTS ---
const AnimatedToggle = ({ open, size = 32 }) => (
  <div
    className="relative flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 cursor-pointer bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-[0px_0px_0px_0px_black] transition-all"
    style={{ width: size, height: size }}
  >
    {open ? <Minimize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" /> : <Maximize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />}
  </div>
);

const MainToolbox = ({ title, icon: Icon, themeColor, children, defaultOpen = true }) => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(defaultOpen);
  return (
    <div className="w-full bg-white flex flex-col overflow-hidden relative shadow-[12px_12px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.8)] transition-all mb-12" style={{ border: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black`, borderRadius: `${CONFIG.radius}px` }}>
      <header onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)} className="h-[80px] min-h-[80px] flex items-center justify-between select-none z-30 relative cursor-pointer" style={{ backgroundColor: themeColor, borderBottom: isOpen ? `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` : "0px" }}>
        <div className="flex items-center h-full flex-1">
          <div className="h-full w-[80px] flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 bg-white" style={{ borderRight: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` }}>
            <Icon size={40} strokeWidth={2.5} className="text-black" />
          </div>
          <h2 className="text-[32px] sm:text-[40px] md:text-[50px] font-[1000] uppercase tracking-tighter leading-none pl-6 truncate text-black">{title}</h2>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center pr-6 h-full"><AnimatedToggle open={isOpen} size={44} /></div>
      </header>
      <div className={`grid transition-[grid-template-rows] duration-500 ease-in-out ${isOpen ? "grid-rows-[1fr]" : "grid-rows-[0fr]"}`}>
        <div className="overflow-hidden min-h-0 bg-neutral-100 p-4 sm:p-6 lg:p-8 space-y-6">{children}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const SubToolbox = ({ title, icon: Icon, headerBg, iconBg, children }) => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(true);
  return (
    <div className="w-full bg-white overflow-hidden relative flex flex-col shrink-0 transition-all duration-300 shadow-[6px_6px_0px_0px_black]" style={{ border: `${CONFIG.stroke}px solid black`, borderRadius: `${CONFIG.radius}px` }}>
      <header onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)} className="flex items-center justify-between select-none relative z-20 cursor-pointer h-[56px] min-h-[56px]" style={{ backgroundColor: headerBg, borderBottom: isOpen ? `${CONFIG.stroke}px solid black` : "0px" }}>
        <div className="flex items-center h-full flex-1">
          <div className="h-full w-[56px] flex items-center justify-center shrink-0" style={{ backgroundColor: iconBg, borderRight: `${CONFIG.stroke}px solid black` }}>
            <Icon size={28} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />
          </div>
          <h3 className="font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black leading-none text-[28px] mt-1 pl-4 pointer-events-none select-none">{title}</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center pr-4 h-full"><AnimatedToggle open={isOpen} size={28} /></div>
      </header>
      <div className={`grid transition-[grid-template-rows] duration-500 ${isOpen ? "grid-rows-[1fr]" : "grid-rows-[0fr]"}`}>
        <div className="overflow-hidden min-h-0"><main className="bg-[#f3f4f6] w-full p-4 md:p-6 text-black flex flex-col gap-6">{children}</main></div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const ComponentShowcase = ({ title, layout = "single", children }) => {
  const layoutClasses = { single: "grid-cols-1", pair: "grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2", grid: "grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-4" };
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
      <div className="h-8 border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg bg-white px-3 inline-flex items-center self-start shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black]">
        <span className="text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">{title}</span>
      </div>
      <div className={`grid ${layoutClasses[layout]} gap-6 w-full`}>{children}</div>
    </div>
  );
};

const VariantLabel = ({ type }) => (
  <div className={`absolute -top-3 -right-3 px-3 py-1 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest z-20 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] ${type === "Tokyo-Pop" ? "bg-[#B28DFF] text-black" : "bg-[#FFE357] text-black"}`}>
    {type}
  </div>
);

// --- 1. CONTROL PACK (Sliders, Toggles, Checkboxes) ---

const SlidersPack = () => {
  const [h1, setH1] = useState(50);
  const [v1, setV1] = useState(75);
  const [s1, setS1] = useState(2);
  const [h2, setH2] = useState(80);
  const [v2, setV2] = useState(40);
  const [s2, setS2] = useState(4);

  return (
    <ComponentShowcase title="6 Slider Variants" layout="pair">

      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col justify-center h-40 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">

        <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={h1} onChange={(e)=>setH1(e.target.value)} className="w-full h-4 bg-[#f3f4f6] border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none outline-none overflow-hidden cursor-pointer" style={{boxShadow: "inset 0 0 0 1px black", background: `linear-gradient(to right, ${COLORS.lime} ${h1}%, #f3f4f6 ${h1}%)`}} />
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop Horizontal Range */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col justify-center h-40 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#24D3FF]">
        <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-[#24D3FF] mb-3"><span>SYS_OVERRIDE</span><span className="text-[#CCFF00]">{h2}</span></div>
        <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={h2} onChange={(e)=>setH2(e.target.value)} className="w-full h-2 bg-black border-[2px] border-[#FF7497] rounded-none appearance-none outline-none cursor-pointer" style={{background: `linear-gradient(to right, ${COLORS.blue} ${h2}%, black ${h2}%)`}} />
        <div className="flex justify-between mt-2 px-1">{[...Array(10)].map((_,i) => <div key={i} className="w-[2px] h-2 bg-[#B28DFF] opacity-50"/>)}</div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Standard Vertical */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-56 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">
        <div className="text-[11px] font-black uppercase mb-4 w-full text-center">Vertical</div>
        <div className="relative h-32 w-4 bg-[#f3f4f6] border-[3px] border-black rounded-full overflow-hidden flex items-end">
          <div className="w-full bg-[#FF7497] border-t-[3px] border-black transition-all" style={{height: `${v1}%`}} />
          <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={v1} onChange={(e)=>setV1(e.target.value)} className="absolute inset-0 w-32 h-4 -translate-x-[56px] translate-y-[56px] -rotate-90 appearance-none bg-transparent outline-none cursor-pointer" />
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop Vertical */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-56 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#FF7497]">
         <div className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-[#FF7497] mb-4 w-full text-center">LVL_{v2}</div>
         <div className="relative h-32 w-8 bg-black border-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] flex flex-col-reverse items-center justify-start p-1 gap-1">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#CCFF00] opacity-20 transition-all origin-bottom" style={{transform: `scaleY(${v2/100})`}}/>
            {[...Array(10)].map((_,i) => <div key={i} className={`w-full h-2 ${i < v2/10 ? 'bg-[#CCFF00] shadow-[0_0_8px_#CCFF00]' : 'bg-[#1A1A24] border border-[#24D3FF]/30'} transition-all`} />)}
            <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={v2} onChange={(e)=>setV2(e.target.value)} className="absolute inset-0 w-32 h-8 -translate-x-[48px] translate-y-[48px] -rotate-90 appearance-none bg-transparent outline-none cursor-pointer opacity-0" />
         </div>

          {[1,2,3,4,5].map(step => (
            <button key={step} onClick={()=>setS1(step)} className={`relative z-10 w-8 h-8 rounded-full border-[3px] border-black flex items-center justify-center text-[10px] font-black transition-all ${s1 >= step ? 'bg-[#FFE357] shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black]' : 'bg-white'}`}>{step}</button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop Step */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col justify-center h-40 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#CCFF00]">

        <div className="flex justify-between relative">
          <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-0 w-full h-[2px] bg-[#B28DFF] -translate-y-1/2 z-0 opacity-50" />
          {[1,2,3,4,5].map(step => (
            <button key={step} onClick={()=>setS2(step)} className={`relative z-10 w-8 h-8 border-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] flex items-center justify-center text-[10px] font-black tracking-widest transition-all ${s2 === step ? 'bg-[#FF7497] text-black shadow-[0_0_15px_#FF7497] scale-110' : 'bg-black text-[#24D3FF]'}`}>{step}</button>
          ))}
        </div>

const HeatgridPack = () => {
  const generateGrid = (rows, cols, isCreative) => {
    let cells = [];
    const colors = isCreative ? ["#1A1A24", "#FF7497", "#B28DFF", "#24D3FF", "#CCFF00"] : ["#ffffff", "#f3f4f6", "#FFE357", "#FCAF57", "#FF7497"];
    for(let r=0; r<rows; r++) {
      for(let c=0; c<cols; c++) {
        const val = Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length);
        cells.push(<div key={`${r}-${c}`} className={`w-full aspect-square border-[2px] border-black rounded-sm shadow-[1px_1px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: colors[val]}} />);
      }
    }
    return cells;
  };

  return (
    <ComponentShowcase title="Data Map: Heatgrids" layout="pair">
      {/* Standard Heatgrid */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col gap-3 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">
        <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
        <div className="text-[11px] font-black uppercase">Activity Map</div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 w-full">{generateGrid(5, 12, false)}</div>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[8px] font-black uppercase mt-1 opacity-60"><span>Jan</span><span>Dec</span></div>
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop Heatgrid */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col gap-3 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#FF7497]">
        <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
        <div className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-[#FF7497]">NODE_DENSITY</div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 w-full">{generateGrid(5, 12, true)}</div>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[8px] font-black uppercase mt-1 text-[#24D3FF] tracking-widest"><span>T-MINUS</span><span>T-ZERO</span></div>
      </div>
    </ComponentShowcase>
  );
};

// --- 3. DATA MATRIX PACK (Complex Table) ---

const ResearchTablePack = () => {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState({ 1: true });
  const [sortOrder, setSortOrder] = useState('desc');

  const data = [
    { id: 1, name: "UX Study Alpha", status: "Active", score: 94, sub: "Tested 40 users. Heatmap shows 80% scroll depth." },
    { id: 2, name: "Beta Conversion", status: "Paused", score: 62, sub: "Requires UI refresh. CTR dropped 15%." },
    { id: 3, name: "Omega Testing", status: "Active", score: 88, sub: "Validating new Neo-Brutal components." },
  ];

  const sortedData = [...data].sort((a,b) => sortOrder === 'desc' ? b.score - a.score : a.score - b.score);

  return (
    <ComponentShowcase title="Complex Research Table" layout="single">
      {/* Standard Table */}
      <div className="border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] overflow-hidden mb-6">
        <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="bg-[#FFE357] border-b-[4px] border-black p-3 grid grid-cols-12 items-center gap-2 text-[11px] font-black uppercase">
          <div className="col-span-1"></div>
          <div className="col-span-5">Project Name</div>
          <div className="col-span-3">Status</div>
          <div className="col-span-3 flex items-center gap-1 cursor-pointer hover:bg-black/10 p-1 rounded-md" onClick={()=>setSortOrder(sortOrder==='desc'?'asc':'desc')}>
            Score {sortOrder === 'desc' ? <ChevronDown size={14}/> : <ChevronUp size={14}/>}
          </div>
        </div>
        {/* Body */}
        <div className="divide-y-[3px] divide-black">
          {sortedData.map((row) => (
            <React.Fragment key={row.id}>
              {/* Main Row */}
              <div className="bg-white p-3 grid grid-cols-12 items-center gap-2 text-[12px] font-bold hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors">
                <div className="col-span-1 flex justify-center cursor-pointer" onClick={()=>setExpanded({...expanded, [row.id]: !expanded[row.id]})}>
                  {expanded[row.id] ? <ChevronDown size={18}/> : <ChevronRight size={18}/>}
                </div>
                <div className="col-span-5 truncate">{row.name}</div>
                <div className="col-span-3 flex items-center gap-2">
                  <div className={`w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black rounded-full ${row.status === 'Active' ? 'bg-[#CCFF00]' : 'bg-[#FF7497]'}`} />
                  <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-black">{row.status}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="col-span-3 flex items-center justify-between">
                  <span className="font-black text-lg leading-none">{row.score}</span>
                  <div className="flex gap-1">
                    <button className="w-8 h-8 bg-[#24D3FF] border-[2px] border-black rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-none"><Edit2 size={12}/></button>
                    <button className="w-8 h-8 bg-[#FF7497] border-[2px] border-black rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-none"><Trash2 size={12}/></button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* Nested Row */}
              {expanded[row.id] && (
                <div className="bg-[#f3f4f6] p-4 border-t-[2px] border-dashed border-black/30">
                  <div className="ml-8 border-[3px] border-black bg-white p-3 rounded-xl shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black]">
                    <span className="text-[9px] font-black uppercase text-black/50 block mb-1">Details_Log</span>
                    <p className="text-[11px] font-bold">{row.sub}</p>
                    <button className="mt-3 px-3 py-1 bg-black text-white text-[9px] font-black uppercase rounded-md shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_#CCFF00]">View Full Report</button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </React.Fragment>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </ComponentShowcase>
  );
};

const ChevronLeftIcon = () => <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="3" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"><path d="m15 18-6-6 6-6"/></svg>;

// --- 6. COMPLEXITY PACK (OTP, Color Picker, Video Player) ---

const OTPPack = () => {
  const [code1, setCode1] = useState(Array(6).fill(''));
  const [code2, setCode2] = useState(Array(6).fill(''));
  const inputs1 = useRef([]);
  const inputs2 = useRef([]);

  const handleChange = (e, index, isCreative) => {
    const val = e.target.value.slice(-1);
    if(isCreative) {
      const newCode = [...code2]; newCode[index] = val; setCode2(newCode);
      if(val && index < 5) inputs2.current[index+1].focus();
    } else {
      const newCode = [...code1]; newCode[index] = val; setCode1(newCode);
      if(val && index < 5) inputs1.current[index+1].focus();
    }
  };

  return (
    <ComponentShowcase title="6-Digit OTP Inputs" layout="pair">
      {/* Standard OTP */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col justify-center items-center h-48 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">
        <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
        <span className="text-[12px] font-black uppercase mb-4">Enter Auth Code</span>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          {code1.map((num, i) => (
            <input key={i} ref={el => inputs1.current[i] = el} type="text" value={num} onChange={(e)=>handleChange(e,i,false)} className="w-10 h-14 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#f3f4f6] text-center text-xl font-black shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black] focus:bg-[#FFE357] focus:outline-none transition-colors" />
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop OTP */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col justify-center items-center h-48 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#FF7497]">
        <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
        <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-[#FF7497] mb-4">DECRYPTION_KEY</span>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          {code2.map((num, i) => (
            <input key={i} ref={el => inputs2.current[i] = el} type="text" value={num} onChange={(e)=>handleChange(e,i,true)} className="w-10 h-14 border-[2px] border-transparent border-b-[#24D3FF] bg-black text-center text-xl font-mono text-[#CCFF00] shadow-[0_4px_0_0_rgba(36,211,255,0.2)] focus:border-[#CCFF00] focus:shadow-[0_4px_0_0_#CCFF00] focus:outline-none transition-all" />
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </ComponentShowcase>
  );
};

const ColorPickerPack = () => {
  const [activeColor1, setActiveColor1] = useState(COLORS.lime);
  const [activeColor2, setActiveColor2] = useState(COLORS.pink);
  
  const stdColors = [COLORS.lime, COLORS.pink, COLORS.blue, COLORS.yellow, COLORS.orange, "#ffffff", "#000000", "#9ca3af"];
  const tpColors = ["#CCFF00", "#FF7497", "#24D3FF", "#B28DFF", "#FF0055", "#00FF9D", "#7000FF", "#1A1A24"];

  return (
    <ComponentShowcase title="Color Swatch Pickers" layout="pair">
      {/* Standard Swatch */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col justify-between h-56 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">
        <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
        <div className="flex gap-4">
          <div className="w-16 h-16 border-[4px] border-black rounded-2xl shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] transition-colors" style={{backgroundColor: activeColor1}}/>
          <div className="flex flex-col justify-center">
             <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase">Selected Hex</span>
             <span className="text-xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter">{activeColor1}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mt-4">
          {stdColors.map(c => (
            <button key={c} onClick={()=>setActiveColor1(c)} className={`w-full aspect-square border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg transition-transform ${activeColor1===c ? 'scale-110 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] z-10' : 'hover:scale-105'}`} style={{backgroundColor: c}}/>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* Tokyo-Pop Swatch */}
      <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col justify-between h-56 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#CCFF00]">
        <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
        <div className="flex gap-4 items-center border-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] p-2 bg-black">
          <div className="w-10 h-10 border-[2px] border-black shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(255,255,255,0.2)] transition-colors" style={{backgroundColor: activeColor2, boxShadow: `0 0 15px ${activeColor2}`}}/>
          <span className="text-lg font-mono text-white tracking-widest">{activeColor2}</span>
        </div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mt-4">
          {tpColors.map(c => (
            <button key={c} onClick={()=>setActiveColor2(c)} className={`w-full h-8 border-[2px] border-black transition-all ${activeColor2===c ? 'shadow-[0_0_10px_white] scale-105 z-10' : 'opacity-60 hover:opacity-100'}`} style={{backgroundColor: c}}/>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </ComponentShowcase>
  );
};

const AdvancedControlsPack = () => {
  const [rating, setRating] = useState(3);
  const [hoverRating, setHoverRating] = useState(0);
  const [tags, setTags] = useState(["BRUTAL", "REACT", "UI"]);

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-12">
      <ComponentShowcase title="Ratings & Interactive Tags" layout="pair">
        {/* Standard Interactive Rating */}
        <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white flex flex-col justify-center items-center h-40 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]">
          <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
          <span className="text-[12px] font-black uppercase mb-4">Rate Component</span>
          <div className="flex gap-2">
            {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((star) => (
              <Star 
                key={star} 
                size={36} 
                strokeWidth={2.5}
                className={`cursor-pointer transition-transform hover:scale-125 ${star <= (hoverRating || rating) ? 'fill-[#FFE357] text-black drop-shadow-[2px_2px_0px_black]' : 'fill-white text-black opacity-30 drop-shadow-[2px_2px_0px_black]'}`}
                onMouseEnter={() => setHoverRating(star)}
                onMouseLeave={() => setHoverRating(0)}
                onClick={() => setRating(star)}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
          <span className="text-[9px] font-black uppercase mt-3 opacity-50">Current: {rating} / 5</span>
        </div>

        {/* Tokyo-Pop Tags Input */}
        <div className="relative p-6 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl bg-[#1A1A24] flex flex-col justify-center h-40 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#B28DFF]">

          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {tags.map((tag, i) => (
              <div key={i} className="flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1 bg-black border-[2px] border-[#FF7497] text-white text-[9px] font-mono shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(255,116,151,0.5)]">
                {tag}
                <X size={12} className="cursor-pointer text-[#FF7497] hover:text-[#CCFF00]" onClick={() => setTags(tags.filter((_, index) => index !== i))} />
              </div>
            ))}
            <button className="px-3 py-1 bg-transparent border-[2px] border-dashed border-[#24D3FF] text-[#24D3FF] text-[9px] font-mono hover:bg-[#24D3FF] hover:text-black transition-colors">

          <VariantLabel type="Standard" />

// --- CORE STRUCTURAL COMPONENTS ---

const VariantLabel = ({ type }) => {
  let styles = "bg-[#FFE357] text-black";
  if (type === "Tokyo-Pop") styles = "bg-[#B28DFF] text-black";
  if (type === "Neo-Tokyo") styles = "bg-white text-black border-[3px] border-black shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_#24D3FF]";
  return (
    <div className={`absolute -top-3 -right-3 px-3 py-1 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest z-20 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center gap-1 ${styles}`}>
      {type === "Neo-Tokyo" && <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full mr-1 animate-pulse" />}{type}
    </div>
  );
};

const AnimatedToggle = ({ open, size = 32 }) => (
  <div className="relative flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 cursor-pointer bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-[0px_0px_0px_0px_black] transition-all" style={{ width: size, height: size }}>
    {open ? <Minimize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" /> : <Maximize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />}
  </div>
);

const MainToolbox = ({ title, icon: Icon, themeColor, children, defaultOpen = true }) => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(defaultOpen);
  return (
    <div className="w-full bg-white flex flex-col overflow-hidden relative shadow-[16px_16px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.8)] transition-all mb-16" style={{ border: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black`, borderRadius: `${CONFIG.radius}px` }}>
      <header onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)} className="h-[80px] min-h-[80px] flex items-center justify-between select-none z-30 relative cursor-pointer" style={{ backgroundColor: themeColor, borderBottom: isOpen ? `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` : "0px" }}>
        <div className="flex items-center h-full flex-1">
          <div className="h-full w-[80px] flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 bg-white" style={{ borderRight: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` }}><Icon size={40} strokeWidth={2.5} className="text-black" /></div>
          <h2 className="text-[32px] sm:text-[40px] md:text-[50px] font-[1000] uppercase tracking-tighter leading-none pl-6 truncate text-black">{title}</h2>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center pr-6 h-full"><AnimatedToggle open={isOpen} size={44} /></div>
      </header>
      <div className={`grid transition-[grid-template-rows] duration-500 ease-in-out ${isOpen ? "grid-rows-[1fr]" : "grid-rows-[0fr]"}`}>
        <div className="overflow-hidden min-h-0 bg-neutral-200 p-4 sm:p-6 lg:p-8 space-y-8">{children}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

};

const ComponentShowcase = ({ title, layout = "single", children }) => {
  const layoutClasses = { 
    single: "grid-cols-1", pair: "grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2", triple: "grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-3", grid: "grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-3 gap-6" 
  };
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
      <div className="h-8 border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg bg-white px-3 inline-flex items-center self-start shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black]"><span className="text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">{title}</span></div>
      <div className={`grid ${layoutClasses[layout]} gap-6 w-full`}>{children}</div>
    </div>
  );
};

const AdvancedRotaryDial = ({ label, targetVal, currentVal, onChange }) => {
  const dialRef = useRef(null);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [startY, setStartY] = useState(0);

  const handlePointerDown = (e) => {
    setIsDragging(true);
    setStartY(e.clientY);
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const handlePointerMove = (e) => {
      if (isDragging) {
        const delta = startY - e.clientY;
        let newVal = currentVal + delta;
        if (newVal > 100) newVal = 100;
        if (newVal < 0) newVal = 0;
        onChange(newVal);
        setStartY(e.clientY);
      }
    };
    const handlePointerUp = () => setIsDragging(false);

    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove);
      window.addEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp);
    }
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove);
      window.removeEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp);
    };
  }, [isDragging, startY, currentVal, onChange]);

  const rotation = (currentVal / 100) * 270 - 135; // Map 0-100 to -135deg to +135deg

  return (
    <div className="relative p-4 border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] flex flex-col items-center h-48 select-none">
      <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black bg-[#CCFF00] px-2 border-[2px] border-black absolute top-2 left-2 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black]">{label}</span>
      <div 
        ref={dialRef}
        onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
        className="w-24 h-24 mt-4 rounded-full border-[6px] border-black bg-gray-200 shadow-[inset_0px_0px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5),4px_4px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center justify-center cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors"
        style={{ transform: `rotate(${rotation}deg)` }}
      >
        <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full border-[2px] border-dashed border-black/30" />
        <div className="absolute top-2 w-3 h-3 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full border-[2px] border-black shadow-[0_0_5px_#FF7497]" />
      </div>
      <div className="w-full flex justify-between mt-4 px-2 text-[10px] font-black font-mono">
        <span className="opacity-50">MIN</span>
        <span className={`${currentVal === targetVal ? 'text-[#24D3FF] scale-125' : 'text-black'} transition-all`}>{Math.round(currentVal)}</span>
        <span className="opacity-50">MAX</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const RubeGoldbergPuzzle = () => {
  // Puzzle State
  const [switches, setSwitches] = useState([false, true, false]);
  const targetSwitches = [true, false, true];
  const isPowerRouted = switches.every((v, i) => v === targetSwitches[i]);

  const [pressure, setPressure] = useState(0);
  const isPressureMaxed = pressure >= 100;

  const [dialVal, setDialVal] = useState(0);
  const targetDial = 88;
  const isDialTuned = Math.abs(dialVal - targetDial) < 2; // within 2 units

  const isCoreUnlocked = isPowerRouted && isPressureMaxed && isDialTuned;
  const [launched, setLaunched] = useState(false);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-3 border-[6px] border-black rounded-[32px] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[16px_16px_0px_0px_#CCFF00] overflow-hidden flex flex-col p-6 relative min-h-[500px]">
      <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 w-32 h-full bg-[repeating-linear-gradient(45deg,transparent,transparent_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_20px)] pointer-events-none" />
      
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center border-b-[4px] border-[#24D3FF] pb-4 mb-6">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-black border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] rounded-full flex items-center justify-center"><Cpu size={24} className="text-[#CCFF00]" /></div>
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-widest text-white leading-none">THE CORE</h3>
            <p className="text-[10px] font-mono text-[#24D3FF] mt-1">SEQ_UNLOCK_REQUIRED</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className={`px-4 py-2 border-[3px] border-black font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-sm ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'bg-[#CCFF00] text-black shadow-[0_0_15px_#CCFF00]' : 'bg-black text-[#FF7497]'}`}>
          {isCoreUnlocked ? 'UNLOCKED' : 'LOCKED'}
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-6 relative z-10 flex-1">
        {/* Step 1: Sequence Toggles */}
        <div className="flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0" /> {/* Wire */}
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-white px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">1. ROUTE POWER</span>
          <div className="flex justify-around mt-2">
            {[0, 1, 2].map((i) => (
              <button 
                key={i} 
                onClick={() => setSwitches(prev => { const n = [...prev]; n[i] = !n[i]; return n; })}
                className="w-10 h-16 bg-gray-200 border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg relative shadow-[inset_0_4px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.2)]"
              >
                <div className={`absolute left-0 right-0 h-8 border-[3px] border-black rounded-md transition-all duration-200 ${switches[i] ? 'top-0 bg-[#CCFF00]' : 'bottom-0 bg-[#FF7497]'}`} />
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black ${isPowerRouted ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-500'}`}>{isPowerRouted ? 'ROUTED' : 'MISMATCH'}</div>
        </div>

        {/* Step 2: Pressure Slider */}
        <div className={`flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 transition-opacity relative ${!isPowerRouted ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0 hidden lg:block" /> {/* Wire */}
          <div className="absolute left-1/2 -bottom-3 w-2 h-6 bg-black z-0 lg:hidden" /> {/* Wire Mobile */}
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-[#24D3FF] px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">2. MAX PRESSURE</span>
          <div className="flex-1 flex items-center">
             <input 
               type="range" min="0" max="100" 
               value={pressure} onChange={(e) => setPressure(parseInt(e.target.value))}
               className="w-full h-8 bg-black/10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none cursor-pointer"
               style={{background: `linear-gradient(to right, #FF7497 ${pressure}%, transparent ${pressure}%)`}}
             />
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black ${isPressureMaxed ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-black'}`}>{pressure}%</div>
        </div>

        {/* Step 3: Dial */}
        <div className={`flex-1 transition-opacity ${!isPressureMaxed ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
           <AdvancedRotaryDial label="3. TUNE TO 88" targetVal={targetDial} currentVal={dialVal} onChange={setDialVal} />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Step 4: Big Launch Button */}
      <div className={`mt-8 pt-8 border-t-[4px] border-dashed border-[#24D3FF]/30 flex flex-col items-center justify-center relative transition-all ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'scale-100 opacity-100' : 'scale-95 opacity-50 pointer-events-none'}`}>
        {launched && (
           <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#CCFF00] z-20 flex items-center justify-center animate-pulse rounded-2xl border-[6px] border-black">
             <h2 className="text-4xl font-[1000] text-black tracking-tighter uppercase">CORE INITIATED</h2>
           </div>
        )}
        <button 
          onClick={() => setLaunched(true)}
          className={`w-32 h-32 rounded-full border-[8px] border-black flex items-center justify-center shadow-[0_15px_0_0_black,0_0_30px_#FF7497] transition-all hover:translate-y-2 hover:shadow-[0_10px_0_0_black,0_0_40px_#FF7497] active:translate-y-4 active:shadow-[0_0px_0_0_black] relative group bg-[#FF7497]`}
        >
          <div className="absolute inset-0 rounded-full bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_left,rgba(255,255,255,0.4),transparent_60%)] pointer-events-none" />
          <Power size={48} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black relative z-10 group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform" />
        </button>
        <span className="text-white font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-6 text-sm">4. INITIATE</span>
      </div>

    </div>
  );
};

// --- EXISTING COMPONENTS (Local wrappers etc) ---
// ... (Keeping LocalSlider, LocalToggle, LocalOTP, Heatgrid, callGeminiAPI, AITitleGenerator, AITerminalAssistant identical to previous to preserve functionality)

const LocalSlider = ({ type, color, label, max, val, bg }) => {
  const [v, setV] = useState(val);
  if (type === "horiz") {
    return (
      <div className={`relative p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: bg}}>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[11px] font-black uppercase mb-3 text-current"><span>{label}</span><span>{v}%</span></div>
        <input type="range" min="0" max={max} value={v} onChange={(e)=>setV(e.target.value)} className="w-full h-4 bg-black/10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none outline-none cursor-pointer" style={{boxShadow: "inset 0 0 0 1px black", background: `linear-gradient(to right, ${color} ${v}%, transparent ${v}%)`}} />
      </div>
    );
  }
  if (type === "step") {
    return (
      <div className={`relative p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: bg}}>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[11px] font-black uppercase mb-4 text-current"><span>{label}</span><span>T-{v}</span></div>
        <div className="flex justify-between relative">
          <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-0 w-full h-2 bg-black/80 -translate-y-1/2 rounded-full z-0" />
          {[1,2,3,4,5].map(s => (
            <button key={s} onClick={()=>setV(s)} className={`relative z-10 w-8 h-8 rounded-full border-[3px] border-black flex items-center justify-center text-[10px] font-black transition-all ${v >= s ? 'shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black]' : 'bg-white text-black'}`} style={{backgroundColor: v >= s ? color : 'white', color: v >= s ? 'black' : 'black'}}>{s}</button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
  return null;
};

const LocalToggle = ({ label, color, bg }) => {
  const [on, setOn] = useState(false);
  return (
    <button onClick={()=>setOn(!on)} className={`p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex items-center justify-between group shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: bg}}>
      <span className="text-[12px] font-black uppercase text-current">{label}</span>
      <div className={`w-14 h-7 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full relative transition-colors ${on ? '' : 'bg-black/10'}`} style={{backgroundColor: on ? color : ''}}>
        <div className={`absolute top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-5 h-5 bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-full shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] transition-all ${on ? 'left-[calc(100%-24px)]' : 'left-[2px]'}`} />
      </div>
    </button>
  );
};

const LocalOTP = ({ dark }) => {
  const [code, setCode] = useState(['4','8','1','5']);
  return (
    <div className={`p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col justify-center items-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_${dark?'#FF7497':'black'}]`} style={{backgroundColor: dark?'#1A1A24':'white'}}>
      <span className={`text-[10px] font-black uppercase mb-3 ${dark?'text-[#FF7497] tracking-widest':'text-black'}`}>{dark?'DECRYPT_KEY':'Auth Code'}</span>
      <div className="flex gap-2">
        {code.map((num, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`w-10 h-12 border-[${dark?'2px':'3px'}] border-black rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-xl font-black ${dark?'bg-black text-[#CCFF00] border-b-[#24D3FF] border-transparent shadow-[0_4px_0_0_rgba(36,211,255,0.2)] font-mono':'bg-[#f3f4f6] text-black shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black]'}`}>{num}</div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const Heatgrid = ({ dark }) => {
  let colors = dark ? ["#1A1A24", "#FF7497", "#B28DFF", "#24D3FF", "#CCFF00"] : ["#ffffff", "#f3f4f6", "#FFE357", "#FCAF57", "#FF7497"];
  return (
    <div className={`relative p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-2 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_${dark?'#FF7497':'black'}]`} style={{backgroundColor: dark?'#1A1A24':'white'}}>
      <div className={`text-[10px] font-black uppercase ${dark?'tracking-widest text-[#FF7497]':'text-black'}`}>{dark?'NODE_DENSITY':'Activity Map'}</div>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 w-full">
        {[...Array(36)].map((_, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`w-full aspect-square ${dark?'':'border-[2px] border-black shadow-[1px_1px_0px_0px_black]'}`} style={{backgroundColor: colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)]}} />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const callGeminiAPI = async (prompt, systemInstruction = null) => {
  const apiKey = ""; 
  const url = `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash-preview-09-2025:generateContent?key=${apiKey}`;
  const payload = { contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }] };
  if (systemInstruction) payload.systemInstruction = { parts: [{ text: systemInstruction }] };
  let retries = 5, delay = 1000;
  while (retries > 0) {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(url, { method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" }, body: JSON.stringify(payload) });
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
      const result = await response.json();
      const text = result?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
      return text ? String(text) : "Error: No text generated.";
    } catch (error) {
      retries -= 1;
      if (retries === 0) return `[ERR_FATAL] API call failed: ${error.message}`;
      await new Promise(res => setTimeout(res, delay));
      delay *= 2;
    }
  }
};

const AITitleGenerator = () => {
  const [concept, setConcept] = useState("");
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [results, setResults] = useState("");

  const handleGenerate = async () => {
    if (!concept) return;
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are a hyper-creative YouTube strategist. The user gives you a video concept. Generate 3 highly engaging, clickable YouTube video titles and a 1-sentence hook for each. Format the output cleanly with bullet points. DO NOT use markdown headers, just plain text with numbers and dashes.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(`Video concept: ${concept}`, systemPrompt);
    setResults(String(response));
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[4px] border-black rounded-2xl bg-[#FFE357] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-6 flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 border-b-[4px] border-black pb-4">
        <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]"><Sparkles size={24} strokeWidth={3} className="text-[#FF7497]" /></div>
        <div><h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black leading-none">AI Idea Studio</h3><p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black/60 mt-1">Powered by Gemini API</p></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-4">
        <input type="text" value={concept} onChange={(e) => setConcept(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter rough video concept..." className="flex-1 h-14 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl pl-4 pr-4 font-black uppercase text-sm outline-none focus:bg-white transition-colors shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] bg-[#f3f4f6]" />
        <button onClick={handleGenerate} disabled={loading || !concept} className="h-14 px-8 bg-[#CCFF00] border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] hover:-translate-y-1 hover:shadow-[4px_6px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-1 active:shadow-none transition-all flex items-center justify-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50">
          {loading ? <Loader2 size={20} className="animate-spin" strokeWidth={3}/> : <Sparkles size={20} strokeWidth={3} />}
          <span className="text-lg font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black mt-0.5">{loading ? "PROCESSING..." : "✨ GENERATE"}</span>
        </button>
      </div>
      {results && <div className="mt-2 bg-white border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl p-4 shadow-[inset_4px_4px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.1)]"><pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap font-bold text-sm leading-relaxed text-black/80 font-sans">{String(results)}</pre></div>}
    </div>
  );
};

const AITerminalAssistant = () => {
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const [log, setLog] = useState([{ role: "system", text: "INITIALIZING SYS_AI_CORE... ONLINE. WAITING FOR PROMPT." }]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const logEndRef = useRef(null);

  const handleCommand = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
    const userCmd = input; setInput("");
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "user", text: String(userCmd) }]);
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are NODE_BRAIN, an aggressive, cyber-punk AI mainframe inside a Neo-Tokyo hacking dashboard. Keep responses brief, edgy, and use technical jargon. End every response with '[EOF]'.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(userCmd, systemPrompt);
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "ai", text: String(response) }]);
    setLoading(false);
  };
  useEffect(() => { logEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" }); }, [log, loading]);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_#24D3FF] overflow-hidden flex flex-col h-[400px] relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
      <div className="bg-[#24D3FF] text-black border-b-[3px] border-black p-2 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2"><Bot size={16} strokeWidth={3} /><span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-0.5">SYS_AI_CORE v2.5</span></div>
        <div className="flex gap-1"><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-white" /><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-black" /></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex-1 p-4 overflow-y-auto font-mono text-[11px] leading-relaxed custom-scrollbar flex flex-col gap-2">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none opacity-5 bg-[linear-gradient(transparent_50%,rgba(0,0,0,0.5)_50%)] bg-[length:100%_4px]" />
        {log.map((entry, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`flex gap-2 relative z-10 ${entry.role === 'user' ? 'text-[#CCFF00]' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'text-[#FF7497]' : 'text-[#24D3FF]'}`}>
            <span className="shrink-0">{entry.role === 'user' ? 'USR>' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'SYS>' : 'AI>'}</span><span className="whitespace-pre-wrap">{String(entry.text)}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
        {loading && <div className="flex gap-2 text-[#24D3FF] relative z-10 animate-pulse"><span className="shrink-0">AI{'>'}</span><span>PROCESSING...</span></div>}
        <div ref={logEndRef} />
      </div>
      <form onSubmit={handleCommand} className="h-12 border-t-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] flex items-center bg-black relative z-10">
        <span className="text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-sm pl-4 pr-2">C:\&gt;</span>
        <input type="text" value={input} onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter command query..." className="flex-1 h-full bg-transparent text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-[11px] uppercase tracking-widest outline-none placeholder:text-[#CCFF00]/30" />
        <button type="submit" disabled={loading} className="h-full px-4 border-l-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#24D3FF] text-black hover:bg-white transition-colors flex items-center justify-center disabled:opacity-50">✨ <Send size={14} className="ml-1" strokeWidth={3}/></button>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
};

          </header>

          {/* TOOLBOX 1: LIGHT MODE */}
          <MainToolbox title="Light UI Matrix" icon={Layout} themeColor={COLORS.white}>
            <LightModeMatrix />
          </MainToolbox>

          {/* TOOLBOX 2: DARK MODE */}
          <MainToolbox title="Dark UI Matrix" icon={Terminal} themeColor={COLORS.dark} defaultOpen={false}>
            <DarkModeMatrix />
          </MainToolbox>

          {/* TOOLBOX 3: EXPERIMENTAL VAULT */}
          <MainToolbox title="Hyper-Interactive Vault" icon={ZapIcon} themeColor={COLORS.pink} defaultOpen={true}>
            <ExperimentalVault />
          </MainToolbox>

        </div>
      </div>
    </>
  );
}

const VariantLabel = ({ type }) => {
  let styles = "bg-[#FFE357] text-black";
  if (type === "Tokyo-Pop") styles = "bg-[#B28DFF] text-black";
  if (type === "Neo-Tokyo") styles = "bg-white text-black border-[3px] border-black shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_#24D3FF]";
  return (
    <div className={`absolute -top-3 -right-3 px-3 py-1 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest z-20 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center gap-1 ${styles}`}>
      {type === "Neo-Tokyo" && <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full mr-1 animate-pulse" />}{type}
    </div>
  );
};

  <div className="relative flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 cursor-pointer bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-[0px_0px_0px_0px_black] transition-all" style={{ width: size, height: size }}>
    {open ? <Minimize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" /> : <Maximize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />}
  </div>
);

      <header onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)} className="h-[80px] min-h-[80px] flex items-center justify-between select-none z-30 relative cursor-pointer" style={{ backgroundColor: themeColor, borderBottom: isOpen ? `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` : "0px" }}>
        <div className="flex items-center h-full flex-1">
          <div className="h-full w-[80px] flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 bg-white" style={{ borderRight: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` }}><Icon size={40} strokeWidth={2.5} className="text-black" /></div>

  return (

      {[...Array(12)].map((_, i) => (
        <div key={i} className="flex-1 flex flex-col justify-end h-full gap-[2px]">
          <div className="w-full bg-[#CCFF00] shadow-[0_0_8px_#CCFF00] origin-bottom transition-all" style={{ height: '100%', animation: `eq-bounce ${0.3 + Math.random()*0.5}s infinite ease-in-out alternate`, animationDelay: `${Math.random()}s` }} />
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
