const AdvancedRotaryDial = ({ label, targetVal, currentVal, onChange }) => {
  const dialRef = useRef(null);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [startY, setStartY] = useState(0);

  const handlePointerDown = (e) => {
    setIsDragging(true);
    setStartY(e.clientY);
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const handlePointerMove = (e) => {
      if (isDragging) {
        const delta = startY - e.clientY;
        let newVal = currentVal + delta;
        if (newVal > 100) newVal = 100;
        if (newVal < 0) newVal = 0;
        onChange(newVal);
        setStartY(e.clientY);
      }
    };
    const handlePointerUp = () => setIsDragging(false);

    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove);
      window.addEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp);
    }
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove);
      window.removeEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp);
    };
  }, [isDragging, startY, currentVal, onChange]);

  const rotation = (currentVal / 100) * 270 - 135; // Map 0-100 to -135deg to +135deg

  return (
    <div className="relative p-4 border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] flex flex-col items-center h-48 select-none">
      <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black bg-[#CCFF00] px-2 border-[2px] border-black absolute top-2 left-2 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black]">{label}</span>
      <div 
        ref={dialRef}
        onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
        className="w-24 h-24 mt-4 rounded-full border-[6px] border-black bg-gray-200 shadow-[inset_0px_0px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5),4px_4px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center justify-center cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors"
        style={{ transform: `rotate(${rotation}deg)` }}
      >
        <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full border-[2px] border-dashed border-black/30" />
        <div className="absolute top-2 w-3 h-3 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full border-[2px] border-black shadow-[0_0_5px_#FF7497]" />
      </div>
      <div className="w-full flex justify-between mt-4 px-2 text-[10px] font-black font-mono">
        <span className="opacity-50">MIN</span>
        <span className={`${currentVal === targetVal ? 'text-[#24D3FF] scale-125' : 'text-black'} transition-all`}>{Math.round(currentVal)}</span>
        <span className="opacity-50">MAX</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const RubeGoldbergPuzzle = () => {
  // Puzzle State
  const [switches, setSwitches] = useState([false, true, false]);
  const targetSwitches = [true, false, true];
  const isPowerRouted = switches.every((v, i) => v === targetSwitches[i]);

  const [pressure, setPressure] = useState(0);
  const isPressureMaxed = pressure >= 100;

  const [dialVal, setDialVal] = useState(0);
  const targetDial = 88;
  const isDialTuned = Math.abs(dialVal - targetDial) < 2; // within 2 units

  const isCoreUnlocked = isPowerRouted && isPressureMaxed && isDialTuned;
  const [launched, setLaunched] = useState(false);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-3 border-[6px] border-black rounded-[32px] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[16px_16px_0px_0px_#CCFF00] overflow-hidden flex flex-col p-6 relative min-h-[500px]">
      <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 w-32 h-full bg-[repeating-linear-gradient(45deg,transparent,transparent_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_20px)] pointer-events-none" />
      
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center border-b-[4px] border-[#24D3FF] pb-4 mb-6">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-black border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] rounded-full flex items-center justify-center"><Cpu size={24} className="text-[#CCFF00]" /></div>
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-widest text-white leading-none">THE CORE</h3>
            <p className="text-[10px] font-mono text-[#24D3FF] mt-1">SEQ_UNLOCK_REQUIRED</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className={`px-4 py-2 border-[3px] border-black font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-sm ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'bg-[#CCFF00] text-black shadow-[0_0_15px_#CCFF00]' : 'bg-black text-[#FF7497]'}`}>
          {isCoreUnlocked ? 'UNLOCKED' : 'LOCKED'}
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-6 relative z-10 flex-1">
        {/* Step 1: Sequence Toggles */}
        <div className="flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0" /> {/* Wire */}
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-white px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">1. ROUTE POWER</span>
          <div className="flex justify-around mt-2">
            {[0, 1, 2].map((i) => (
              <button 
                key={i} 
                onClick={() => setSwitches(prev => { const n = [...prev]; n[i] = !n[i]; return n; })}
                className="w-10 h-16 bg-gray-200 border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg relative shadow-[inset_0_4px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.2)]"
              >
                <div className={`absolute left-0 right-0 h-8 border-[3px] border-black rounded-md transition-all duration-200 ${switches[i] ? 'top-0 bg-[#CCFF00]' : 'bottom-0 bg-[#FF7497]'}`} />
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black ${isPowerRouted ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-500'}`}>{isPowerRouted ? 'ROUTED' : 'MISMATCH'}</div>
        </div>

        {/* Step 2: Pressure Slider */}
        <div className={`flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 transition-opacity relative ${!isPowerRouted ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0 hidden lg:block" /> {/* Wire */}
          <div className="absolute left-1/2 -bottom-3 w-2 h-6 bg-black z-0 lg:hidden" /> {/* Wire Mobile */}
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-[#24D3FF] px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">2. MAX PRESSURE</span>
          <div className="flex-1 flex items-center">
             <input 
               type="range" min="0" max="100" 
               value={pressure} onChange={(e) => setPressure(parseInt(e.target.value))}
               className="w-full h-8 bg-black/10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none cursor-pointer"
               style={{background: `linear-gradient(to right, #FF7497 ${pressure}%, transparent ${pressure}%)`}}
             />
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black ${isPressureMaxed ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-black'}`}>{pressure}%</div>
        </div>

        {/* Step 3: Dial */}
        <div className={`flex-1 transition-opacity ${!isPressureMaxed ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
           <AdvancedRotaryDial label="3. TUNE TO 88" targetVal={targetDial} currentVal={dialVal} onChange={setDialVal} />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Step 4: Big Launch Button */}
      <div className={`mt-8 pt-8 border-t-[4px] border-dashed border-[#24D3FF]/30 flex flex-col items-center justify-center relative transition-all ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'scale-100 opacity-100' : 'scale-95 opacity-50 pointer-events-none'}`}>
        {launched && (
           <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#CCFF00] z-20 flex items-center justify-center animate-pulse rounded-2xl border-[6px] border-black">
             <h2 className="text-4xl font-[1000] text-black tracking-tighter uppercase">CORE INITIATED</h2>
           </div>
        )}
        <button 
          onClick={() => setLaunched(true)}
          className={`w-32 h-32 rounded-full border-[8px] border-black flex items-center justify-center shadow-[0_15px_0_0_black,0_0_30px_#FF7497] transition-all hover:translate-y-2 hover:shadow-[0_10px_0_0_black,0_0_40px_#FF7497] active:translate-y-4 active:shadow-[0_0px_0_0_black] relative group bg-[#FF7497]`}
        >
          <div className="absolute inset-0 rounded-full bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_left,rgba(255,255,255,0.4),transparent_60%)] pointer-events-none" />
          <Power size={48} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black relative z-10 group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform" />
        </button>
        <span className="text-white font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-6 text-sm">4. INITIATE</span>
      </div>

    </div>
  );
};

        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#FF7497] transition-all duration-300 ease-out group-hover:clip-path-full" style={{ clipPath: 'polygon(100% 0, 100% 0, 100% 100%, 100% 100%)' }} />
        {/* Hacky way to inject dynamic clip paths on hover via raw CSS class since dynamic inline styles on hover require JS */}
        <style>{`.group:hover > .bg-\\[\\#24D3FF\\] { clip-path: polygon(0 0, 50% 0, 20% 100%, 0% 100%) !important; } .group:hover > .bg-\\[\\#FF7497\\] { clip-path: polygon(100% 0, 50% 0, 80% 100%, 100% 100%) !important; }`}</style>

const LocalSlider = ({ type, color, label, max, val, bg }) => {
  const [v, setV] = useState(val);
  if (type === "horiz") {
    return (
      <div className={`relative p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: bg}}>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[11px] font-black uppercase mb-3 text-current"><span>{label}</span><span>{v}%</span></div>
        <input type="range" min="0" max={max} value={v} onChange={(e)=>setV(e.target.value)} className="w-full h-4 bg-black/10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none outline-none cursor-pointer" style={{boxShadow: "inset 0 0 0 1px black", background: `linear-gradient(to right, ${color} ${v}%, transparent ${v}%)`}} />
      </div>
    );
  }
  if (type === "step") {
    return (
      <div className={`relative p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: bg}}>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[11px] font-black uppercase mb-4 text-current"><span>{label}</span><span>T-{v}</span></div>
        <div className="flex justify-between relative">
          <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-0 w-full h-2 bg-black/80 -translate-y-1/2 rounded-full z-0" />
          {[1,2,3,4,5].map(s => (
            <button key={s} onClick={()=>setV(s)} className={`relative z-10 w-8 h-8 rounded-full border-[3px] border-black flex items-center justify-center text-[10px] font-black transition-all ${v >= s ? 'shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black]' : 'bg-white text-black'}`} style={{backgroundColor: v >= s ? color : 'white', color: v >= s ? 'black' : 'black'}}>{s}</button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
  return null;
};

const LocalToggle = ({ label, color, bg }) => {
  const [on, setOn] = useState(false);
  return (
    <button onClick={()=>setOn(!on)} className={`p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex items-center justify-between group shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: bg}}>
      <span className="text-[12px] font-black uppercase text-current">{label}</span>
      <div className={`w-14 h-7 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full relative transition-colors ${on ? '' : 'bg-black/10'}`} style={{backgroundColor: on ? color : ''}}>
        <div className={`absolute top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-5 h-5 bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-full shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] transition-all ${on ? 'left-[calc(100%-24px)]' : 'left-[2px]'}`} />
      </div>
    </button>
  );
};

const LocalOTP = ({ dark }) => {
  const [code, setCode] = useState(['4','8','1','5']);
  return (
    <div className={`p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col justify-center items-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_${dark?'#FF7497':'black'}]`} style={{backgroundColor: dark?'#1A1A24':'white'}}>
      <span className={`text-[10px] font-black uppercase mb-3 ${dark?'text-[#FF7497] tracking-widest':'text-black'}`}>{dark?'DECRYPT_KEY':'Auth Code'}</span>
      <div className="flex gap-2">
        {code.map((num, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`w-10 h-12 border-[${dark?'2px':'3px'}] border-black rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-xl font-black ${dark?'bg-black text-[#CCFF00] border-b-[#24D3FF] border-transparent shadow-[0_4px_0_0_rgba(36,211,255,0.2)] font-mono':'bg-[#f3f4f6] text-black shadow-[3px_3px_0px_0px_black]'}`}>{num}</div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const Heatgrid = ({ dark }) => {
  let colors = dark ? ["#1A1A24", "#FF7497", "#B28DFF", "#24D3FF", "#CCFF00"] : ["#ffffff", "#f3f4f6", "#FFE357", "#FCAF57", "#FF7497"];
  return (
    <div className={`relative p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-2 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_${dark?'#FF7497':'black'}]`} style={{backgroundColor: dark?'#1A1A24':'white'}}>
      <div className={`text-[10px] font-black uppercase ${dark?'tracking-widest text-[#FF7497]':'text-black'}`}>{dark?'NODE_DENSITY':'Activity Map'}</div>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 w-full">
        {[...Array(36)].map((_, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`w-full aspect-square ${dark?'':'border-[2px] border-black shadow-[1px_1px_0px_0px_black]'}`} style={{backgroundColor: colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)]}} />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const callGeminiAPI = async (prompt, systemInstruction = null) => {
  const apiKey = ""; 
  const url = `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash-preview-09-2025:generateContent?key=${apiKey}`;
  const payload = { contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }] };
  if (systemInstruction) payload.systemInstruction = { parts: [{ text: systemInstruction }] };
  let retries = 5, delay = 1000;
  while (retries > 0) {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(url, { method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" }, body: JSON.stringify(payload) });
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
      const result = await response.json();
      const text = result?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
      return text ? String(text) : "Error: No text generated.";
    } catch (error) {
      retries -= 1;
      if (retries === 0) return `[ERR_FATAL] API call failed: ${error.message}`;
      await new Promise(res => setTimeout(res, delay));
      delay *= 2;
    }
  }
};

const AITitleGenerator = () => {
  const [concept, setConcept] = useState("");
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [results, setResults] = useState("");

  const handleGenerate = async () => {
    if (!concept) return;
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are a hyper-creative YouTube strategist. The user gives you a video concept. Generate 3 highly engaging, clickable YouTube video titles and a 1-sentence hook for each. Format the output cleanly with bullet points. DO NOT use markdown headers, just plain text with numbers and dashes.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(`Video concept: ${concept}`, systemPrompt);
    setResults(String(response));
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[4px] border-black rounded-2xl bg-[#FFE357] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-6 flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 border-b-[4px] border-black pb-4">
        <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]"><Sparkles size={24} strokeWidth={3} className="text-[#FF7497]" /></div>
        <div><h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black leading-none">AI Idea Studio</h3><p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black/60 mt-1">Powered by Gemini API</p></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-4">
        <input type="text" value={concept} onChange={(e) => setConcept(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter rough video concept..." className="flex-1 h-14 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl pl-4 pr-4 font-black uppercase text-sm outline-none focus:bg-white transition-colors shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] bg-[#f3f4f6]" />
        <button onClick={handleGenerate} disabled={loading || !concept} className="h-14 px-8 bg-[#CCFF00] border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] hover:-translate-y-1 hover:shadow-[4px_6px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-1 active:shadow-none transition-all flex items-center justify-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50">
          {loading ? <Loader2 size={20} className="animate-spin" strokeWidth={3}/> : <Sparkles size={20} strokeWidth={3} />}
          <span className="text-lg font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black mt-0.5">{loading ? "PROCESSING..." : "✨ GENERATE"}</span>
        </button>
      </div>
      {results && <div className="mt-2 bg-white border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl p-4 shadow-[inset_4px_4px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.1)]"><pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap font-bold text-sm leading-relaxed text-black/80 font-sans">{String(results)}</pre></div>}
    </div>
  );
};

const AITerminalAssistant = () => {
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const [log, setLog] = useState([{ role: "system", text: "INITIALIZING SYS_AI_CORE... ONLINE. WAITING FOR PROMPT." }]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const logEndRef = useRef(null);

  const handleCommand = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
    const userCmd = input; setInput("");
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "user", text: String(userCmd) }]);
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are NODE_BRAIN, an aggressive, cyber-punk AI mainframe inside a Neo-Tokyo hacking dashboard. Keep responses brief, edgy, and use technical jargon. End every response with '[EOF]'.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(userCmd, systemPrompt);
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "ai", text: String(response) }]);
    setLoading(false);
  };
  useEffect(() => { logEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" }); }, [log, loading]);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_#24D3FF] overflow-hidden flex flex-col h-[400px] relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
      <div className="bg-[#24D3FF] text-black border-b-[3px] border-black p-2 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2"><Bot size={16} strokeWidth={3} /><span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-0.5">SYS_AI_CORE v2.5</span></div>
        <div className="flex gap-1"><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-white" /><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-black" /></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex-1 p-4 overflow-y-auto font-mono text-[11px] leading-relaxed custom-scrollbar flex flex-col gap-2">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none opacity-5 bg-[linear-gradient(transparent_50%,rgba(0,0,0,0.5)_50%)] bg-[length:100%_4px]" />
        {log.map((entry, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`flex gap-2 relative z-10 ${entry.role === 'user' ? 'text-[#CCFF00]' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'text-[#FF7497]' : 'text-[#24D3FF]'}`}>
            <span className="shrink-0">{entry.role === 'user' ? 'USR>' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'SYS>' : 'AI>'}</span><span className="whitespace-pre-wrap">{String(entry.text)}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
        {loading && <div className="flex gap-2 text-[#24D3FF] relative z-10 animate-pulse"><span className="shrink-0">AI{'>'}</span><span>PROCESSING...</span></div>}
        <div ref={logEndRef} />
      </div>
      <form onSubmit={handleCommand} className="h-12 border-t-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] flex items-center bg-black relative z-10">
        <span className="text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-sm pl-4 pr-2">C:\&gt;</span>
        <input type="text" value={input} onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter command query..." className="flex-1 h-full bg-transparent text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-[11px] uppercase tracking-widest outline-none placeholder:text-[#CCFF00]/30" />
        <button type="submit" disabled={loading} className="h-full px-4 border-l-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#24D3FF] text-black hover:bg-white transition-colors flex items-center justify-center disabled:opacity-50">✨ <Send size={14} className="ml-1" strokeWidth={3}/></button>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
};

  return (
    <div className={`absolute -top-3 -right-3 px-3 py-1 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest z-20 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center gap-1 ${styles}`}>
      {type === "Neo-Tokyo" && <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full mr-1 animate-pulse" />}{type}
    </div>
  );
};

const LocalSlider = ({ type, color, label, max, val, bg }) => {
  const [v, setV] = useState(val);
  if (type === "horiz") {
    return (
      <div className={`relative p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: bg}}>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[11px] font-black uppercase mb-3 text-current"><span>{label}</span><span>{v}%</span></div>
        <input type="range" min="0" max={max} value={v} onChange={(e)=>setV(e.target.value)} className="w-full h-4 bg-black/10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none outline-none cursor-pointer" style={{boxShadow: "inset 0 0 0 1px black", background: `linear-gradient(to right, ${color} ${v}%, transparent ${v}%)`}} />
      </div>
    );
  }
  if (type === "step") {
    return (
      <div className={`relative p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]`} style={{backgroundColor: bg}}>
        <div className="flex justify-between text-[11px] font-black uppercase mb-4 text-current"><span>{label}</span><span>T-{v}</span></div>
        <div className="flex justify-between relative">
          <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-0 w-full h-2 bg-black/80 -translate-y-1/2 rounded-full z-0" />
          {[1,2,3,4,5].map(s => (
            <button key={s} onClick={()=>setV(s)} className={`relative z-10 w-8 h-8 rounded-full border-[3px] border-black flex items-center justify-center text-[10px] font-black transition-all ${v >= s ? 'shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black]' : 'bg-white text-black'}`} style={{backgroundColor: v >= s ? color : 'white', color: v >= s ? 'black' : 'black'}}>{s}</button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
  return null;
};

      </div>

const Heatgrid = ({ dark }) => {
  let colors = dark ? ["#1A1A24", "#FF7497", "#B28DFF", "#24D3FF", "#CCFF00"] : ["#ffffff", "#f3f4f6", "#FFE357", "#FCAF57", "#FF7497"];
  return (
    <div className={`relative p-4 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-2 shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_${dark?'#FF7497':'black'}]`} style={{backgroundColor: dark?'#1A1A24':'white'}}>
      <div className={`text-[10px] font-black uppercase ${dark?'tracking-widest text-[#FF7497]':'text-black'}`}>{dark?'NODE_DENSITY':'Activity Map'}</div>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 w-full">
        {[...Array(36)].map((_, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`w-full aspect-square ${dark?'':'border-[2px] border-black shadow-[1px_1px_0px_0px_black]'}`} style={{backgroundColor: colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)]}} />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const callGeminiAPI = async (prompt, systemInstruction = null) => {
  const apiKey = ""; 
  const url = `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash-preview-09-2025:generateContent?key=${apiKey}`;
  const payload = { contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }] };
  if (systemInstruction) payload.systemInstruction = { parts: [{ text: systemInstruction }] };
  let retries = 5, delay = 1000;
  while (retries > 0) {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(url, { method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" }, body: JSON.stringify(payload) });
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
      const result = await response.json();
      const text = result?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
      return text ? String(text) : "Error: No text generated.";
    } catch (error) {
      retries -= 1;
      if (retries === 0) return `[ERR_FATAL] API call failed: ${error.message}`;
      await new Promise(res => setTimeout(res, delay));
      delay *= 2;
    }
  }
};

const AITitleGenerator = () => {
  const [concept, setConcept] = useState("");
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [results, setResults] = useState("");

  const handleGenerate = async () => {
    if (!concept) return;
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are a hyper-creative YouTube strategist. The user gives you a video concept. Generate 3 highly engaging, clickable YouTube video titles and a 1-sentence hook for each. Format the output cleanly with bullet points. DO NOT use markdown headers, just plain text with numbers and dashes.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(`Video concept: ${concept}`, systemPrompt);
    setResults(String(response));
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[4px] border-black rounded-2xl bg-[#FFE357] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-6 flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 border-b-[4px] border-black pb-4">
        <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]"><Sparkles size={24} strokeWidth={3} className="text-[#FF7497]" /></div>
        <div><h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black leading-none">AI Idea Studio</h3><p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black/60 mt-1">Powered by Gemini API</p></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-4">
        <input type="text" value={concept} onChange={(e) => setConcept(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter rough video concept..." className="flex-1 h-14 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl pl-4 pr-4 font-black uppercase text-sm outline-none focus:bg-white transition-colors shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] bg-[#f3f4f6]" />
        <button onClick={handleGenerate} disabled={loading || !concept} className="h-14 px-8 bg-[#CCFF00] border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] hover:-translate-y-1 hover:shadow-[4px_6px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-1 active:shadow-none transition-all flex items-center justify-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50">
          {loading ? <Loader2 size={20} className="animate-spin" strokeWidth={3}/> : <Sparkles size={20} strokeWidth={3} />}
          <span className="text-lg font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black mt-0.5">{loading ? "PROCESSING..." : "✨ GENERATE"}</span>
        </button>
      </div>
      {results && <div className="mt-2 bg-white border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl p-4 shadow-[inset_4px_4px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.1)]"><pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap font-bold text-sm leading-relaxed text-black/80 font-sans">{String(results)}</pre></div>}
    </div>
  );
};

const AITerminalAssistant = () => {
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const [log, setLog] = useState([{ role: "system", text: "INITIALIZING SYS_AI_CORE... ONLINE. WAITING FOR PROMPT." }]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const logEndRef = useRef(null);

  const handleCommand = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
    const userCmd = input; setInput("");
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "user", text: String(userCmd) }]);
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are NODE_BRAIN, an aggressive, cyber-punk AI mainframe inside a Neo-Tokyo hacking dashboard. Keep responses brief, edgy, and use technical jargon. End every response with '[EOF]'.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(userCmd, systemPrompt);
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "ai", text: String(response) }]);
    setLoading(false);
  };
  useEffect(() => { logEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" }); }, [log, loading]);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_#24D3FF] overflow-hidden flex flex-col h-[400px] relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
      <div className="bg-[#24D3FF] text-black border-b-[3px] border-black p-2 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2"><Bot size={16} strokeWidth={3} /><span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-0.5">SYS_AI_CORE v2.5</span></div>
        <div className="flex gap-1"><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-white" /><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-black" /></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex-1 p-4 overflow-y-auto font-mono text-[11px] leading-relaxed custom-scrollbar flex flex-col gap-2">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none opacity-5 bg-[linear-gradient(transparent_50%,rgba(0,0,0,0.5)_50%)] bg-[length:100%_4px]" />
        {log.map((entry, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`flex gap-2 relative z-10 ${entry.role === 'user' ? 'text-[#CCFF00]' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'text-[#FF7497]' : 'text-[#24D3FF]'}`}>
            <span className="shrink-0">{entry.role === 'user' ? 'USR>' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'SYS>' : 'AI>'}</span><span className="whitespace-pre-wrap">{String(entry.text)}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
        {loading && <div className="flex gap-2 text-[#24D3FF] relative z-10 animate-pulse"><span className="shrink-0">AI{'>'}</span><span>PROCESSING...</span></div>}
        <div ref={logEndRef} />
      </div>
      <form onSubmit={handleCommand} className="h-12 border-t-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] flex items-center bg-black relative z-10">
        <span className="text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-sm pl-4 pr-2">C:\&gt;</span>
        <input type="text" value={input} onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter command query..." className="flex-1 h-full bg-transparent text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-[11px] uppercase tracking-widest outline-none placeholder:text-[#CCFF00]/30" />
        <button type="submit" disabled={loading} className="h-full px-4 border-l-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#24D3FF] text-black hover:bg-white transition-colors flex items-center justify-center disabled:opacity-50">✨ <Send size={14} className="ml-1" strokeWidth={3}/></button>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
};

const AdvancedRotaryDial = ({ label, targetVal, currentVal, onChange }) => {
  const dialRef = useRef(null);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [startY, setStartY] = useState(0);

  const handlePointerDown = (e) => {
    setIsDragging(true);
    setStartY(e.clientY);
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const handlePointerMove = (e) => {
      if (isDragging) {
        const delta = startY - e.clientY;
        let newVal = currentVal + delta;
        if (newVal > 100) newVal = 100;
        if (newVal < 0) newVal = 0;
        onChange(newVal);
        setStartY(e.clientY);
      }
    };
    const handlePointerUp = () => setIsDragging(false);

    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove);
      window.addEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp);
    }
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove);
      window.removeEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp);
    };
  }, [isDragging, startY, currentVal, onChange]);

  const rotation = (currentVal / 100) * 270 - 135; 

  return (
    <div className="relative p-4 border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full min-h-[160px] select-none">
      <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black bg-[#CCFF00] px-2 border-[2px] border-black absolute top-2 left-2 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black]">{label}</span>
      <div 
        ref={dialRef}
        onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
        className="w-24 h-24 mt-4 rounded-full border-[6px] border-black bg-gray-200 shadow-[inset_0px_0px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5),4px_4px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center justify-center cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors"
        style={{ transform: `rotate(${rotation}deg)` }}
      >
        <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full border-[2px] border-dashed border-black/30" />
        <div className="absolute top-2 w-3 h-3 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full border-[2px] border-black shadow-[0_0_5px_#FF7497]" />
      </div>
      <div className="w-full flex justify-between mt-4 px-2 text-[10px] font-black font-mono">
        <span className="opacity-50">MIN</span>
        <span className={`${Math.abs(currentVal - targetVal) < 2 ? 'text-[#24D3FF] scale-125' : 'text-black'} transition-all`}>{Math.round(currentVal)}</span>
        <span className="opacity-50">MAX</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const RubeGoldbergPuzzle = () => {
  const [switches, setSwitches] = useState([false, true, false]);
  const targetSwitches = [true, false, true];
  const isPowerRouted = switches.every((v, i) => v === targetSwitches[i]);

  const [pressure, setPressure] = useState(0);
  const isPressureMaxed = pressure >= 100;

  const [dialVal, setDialVal] = useState(0);
  const targetDial = 88;
  const isDialTuned = Math.abs(dialVal - targetDial) < 2; 

  const isCoreUnlocked = isPowerRouted && isPressureMaxed && isDialTuned;
  const [launched, setLaunched] = useState(false);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-8 border-[6px] border-black rounded-[32px] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[16px_16px_0px_0px_#CCFF00] overflow-hidden flex flex-col p-6 relative min-h-[500px]">
      <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 w-32 h-full bg-[repeating-linear-gradient(45deg,transparent,transparent_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_20px)] pointer-events-none" />
      
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center border-b-[4px] border-[#24D3FF] pb-4 mb-6">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-black border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] rounded-full flex items-center justify-center"><Cpu size={24} className="text-[#CCFF00]" /></div>
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-widest text-white leading-none">THE CORE</h3>
            <p className="text-[10px] font-mono text-[#24D3FF] mt-1">SEQ_UNLOCK_REQUIRED</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className={`px-4 py-2 border-[3px] border-black font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-sm ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'bg-[#CCFF00] text-black shadow-[0_0_15px_#CCFF00]' : 'bg-black text-[#FF7497]'}`}>
          {isCoreUnlocked ? 'UNLOCKED' : 'LOCKED'}
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-6 relative z-10 flex-1">
        {/* Step 1: Sequence Toggles */}
        <div className="flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0 hidden md:block" />
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-white px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">1. ROUTE POWER</span>
          <div className="flex justify-around mt-2">
            {[0, 1, 2].map((i) => (
              <button 
                key={i} 
                onClick={() => setSwitches(prev => { const n = [...prev]; n[i] = !n[i]; return n; })}
                className="w-12 h-20 bg-gray-200 border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg relative shadow-[inset_0_4px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.2)]"
              >
                <div className={`absolute left-0 right-0 h-10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-md transition-all duration-200 ${switches[i] ? 'top-0 bg-[#CCFF00]' : 'bottom-0 bg-[#FF7497]'}`} />
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black mt-auto ${isPowerRouted ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-500'}`}>{isPowerRouted ? 'ROUTED' : 'MISMATCH'}</div>
        </div>

        {/* Step 2: Pressure Slider */}
        <div className={`flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 transition-opacity relative ${!isPowerRouted ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0 hidden md:block" /> 
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-[#24D3FF] px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">2. MAX PRESSURE</span>
          <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center">
             <input 
               type="range" min="0" max="100" 
               value={pressure} onChange={(e) => setPressure(parseInt(e.target.value))}
               className="w-full h-8 bg-black/10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none cursor-pointer"
               style={{background: `linear-gradient(to right, #FF7497 ${pressure}%, transparent ${pressure}%)`}}
             />
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black mt-auto ${isPressureMaxed ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-black'}`}>{pressure}%</div>
        </div>

        {/* Step 3: Dial */}
        <div className={`flex-1 transition-opacity ${!isPressureMaxed ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
           <AdvancedRotaryDial label="3. TUNE TO 88" targetVal={targetDial} currentVal={dialVal} onChange={setDialVal} />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Step 4: Big Launch Button */}
      <div className={`mt-8 pt-8 border-t-[4px] border-dashed border-[#24D3FF]/30 flex flex-col items-center justify-center relative transition-all ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'scale-100 opacity-100' : 'scale-95 opacity-50 pointer-events-none'}`}>
        {launched && (
           <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#CCFF00] z-20 flex items-center justify-center animate-pulse rounded-2xl border-[6px] border-black">
             <h2 className="text-4xl font-[1000] text-black tracking-tighter uppercase">CORE INITIATED</h2>
           </div>
        )}
        <button 
          onClick={() => setLaunched(true)}
          className={`w-32 h-32 rounded-full border-[8px] border-black flex items-center justify-center shadow-[0_15px_0_0_black,0_0_30px_#FF7497] transition-all hover:translate-y-2 hover:shadow-[0_10px_0_0_black,0_0_40px_#FF7497] active:translate-y-4 active:shadow-[0_0px_0_0_black] relative group bg-[#FF7497]`}
        >
          <div className="absolute inset-0 rounded-full bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_left,rgba(255,255,255,0.4),transparent_60%)] pointer-events-none" />
          <Power size={48} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black relative z-10 group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform" />
        </button>
        <span className="text-white font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-6 text-sm">4. INITIATE</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const MechaCockpitPack = () => {
  const [eject, setEject] = useState(0);
  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-4">
       <div className="col-span-12 md:col-span-4 h-40 border-[3px] border-black bg-white shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] p-4 flex items-center justify-center relative overflow-hidden group">
         <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase absolute top-2 left-2 bg-[#FFE357] px-1 border-[2px] border-black z-20">RADAR</span>
         <div className="w-24 h-24 rounded-full border-[2px] border-[#CCFF00] bg-black relative overflow-hidden">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 conic-radar animate-radar-spin z-10" />
            <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-1/2 w-full h-[1px] bg-[#CCFF00]/30 -translate-y-1/2 z-0" />
            <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-1/2 h-full w-[1px] bg-[#CCFF00]/30 -translate-x-1/2 z-0" />
         </div>
       </div>
       <div className="col-span-12 md:col-span-4 h-40 border-[3px] border-black bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_#FF7497] p-4 flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
         <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase text-[#FF7497] mb-2">EJECT_SEQ</span>
         <button 
           onClick={() => setEject(e => e < 2 ? e + 1 : 0)} 
           className={`w-20 h-20 border-[4px] border-black rounded-lg transition-all relative ${eject === 0 ? 'bg-stripes shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]' : eject === 1 ? 'bg-black shadow-[inset_0_0_10px_black]' : 'bg-red-600 scale-95 shadow-none'}`}
         >
            {eject === 1 && <div className="absolute inset-2 bg-red-500 rounded border-[2px] border-black hover:bg-red-400" />}
            {eject === 2 && <span className="text-white font-black text-xs absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center animate-pulse">EJECTED</span>}
         </button>
       </div>
       <div className="col-span-12 md:col-span-4 h-40 border-[3px] border-black bg-white shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] p-4 flex gap-4 items-center">
         <div className="h-full w-12 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full bg-gray-200 relative overflow-hidden shadow-[inset_0_0_10px_black]">
           <input type="range" className="absolute inset-0 w-32 h-12 -rotate-90 origin-bottom-left -translate-y-full appearance-none bg-transparent cursor-pointer z-10" />
           <div className="absolute bottom-0 w-full h-[50%] bg-[linear-gradient(0deg,#FF7497,#FFE357)] z-0 transition-all pointer-events-none" />
         </div>
         <span className="text-[14px] font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter w-min leading-tight">THRUSTER LEVER</span>

    </div>
  );
};

const VariantLabel = ({ type }) => {
  let styles = "bg-[#FFE357] text-black";
  if (type === "Tokyo-Pop") styles = "bg-[#B28DFF] text-black";
  if (type === "Neo-Tokyo") styles = "bg-white text-black border-[3px] border-black shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_#24D3FF]";
  return (
    <div className={`absolute -top-3 -right-3 px-3 py-1 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest z-20 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center gap-1 ${styles}`}>
      {type === "Neo-Tokyo" && <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full mr-1 animate-pulse" />}{type}
    </div>
  );
};

const AnimatedToggle = ({ open, size = 32 }) => (
  <div className="relative flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 cursor-pointer bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-[2px] active:shadow-[0px_0px_0px_0px_black] transition-all" style={{ width: size, height: size }}>
    {open ? <Minimize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" /> : <Maximize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />}
  </div>
);

const MainToolbox = ({ title, icon: Icon, themeColor, children, defaultOpen = true }) => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(defaultOpen);
  return (
    <div className="w-full bg-white flex flex-col overflow-hidden relative shadow-[16px_16px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.8)] transition-all mb-16" style={{ border: `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black`, borderRadius: `${CONFIG.radius}px` }}>
      <header onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)} className="h-[80px] min-h-[80px] flex items-center justify-between select-none z-30 relative cursor-pointer" style={{ backgroundColor: themeColor, borderBottom: isOpen ? `${CONFIG.scaffoldStroke}px solid black` : "0px" }}>
        <div className="flex items-center h-full flex-1">

        <div className="overflow-hidden min-h-0 bg-neutral-200 p-4 sm:p-6 lg:p-8 space-y-8">{children}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// --- GEMINI API INTEGRATION ---
const callGeminiAPI = async (prompt, systemInstruction = null) => {
  const apiKey = ""; 
  const url = `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash-preview-09-2025:generateContent?key=${apiKey}`;
  const payload = { contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }] };
  if (systemInstruction) payload.systemInstruction = { parts: [{ text: systemInstruction }] };
  let retries = 5, delay = 1000;
  while (retries > 0) {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(url, { method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" }, body: JSON.stringify(payload) });
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
      const result = await response.json();
      const text = result?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
      return text ? String(text) : "Error: No text generated.";
    } catch (error) {
      retries -= 1;
      if (retries === 0) return `[ERR_FATAL] API call failed: ${error.message}`;
      await new Promise(res => setTimeout(res, delay));
      delay *= 2;
    }
  }
};

const AITitleGenerator = () => {
  const [concept, setConcept] = useState("");
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [results, setResults] = useState("");

  const handleGenerate = async () => {
    if (!concept) return;
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are a hyper-creative YouTube strategist. The user gives you a video concept. Generate 3 highly engaging, clickable YouTube video titles and a 1-sentence hook for each. Format the output cleanly with bullet points. DO NOT use markdown headers, just plain text with numbers and dashes.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(`Video concept: ${concept}`, systemPrompt);
    setResults(String(response));
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[4px] border-black rounded-2xl bg-[#FFE357] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-6 flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 border-b-[4px] border-black pb-4">
        <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]"><Sparkles size={24} strokeWidth={3} className="text-[#FF7497]" /></div>
        <div><h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black leading-none">AI Idea Studio</h3><p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black/60 mt-1">Powered by Gemini API</p></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-4">
        <input type="text" value={concept} onChange={(e) => setConcept(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter rough video concept..." className="flex-1 h-14 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl pl-4 pr-4 font-black uppercase text-sm outline-none focus:bg-white transition-colors shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] bg-[#f3f4f6]" />
        <button onClick={handleGenerate} disabled={loading || !concept} className="h-14 px-8 bg-[#CCFF00] border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] hover:-translate-y-1 hover:shadow-[4px_6px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-1 active:shadow-none transition-all flex items-center justify-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50">
          {loading ? <Loader2 size={20} className="animate-spin" strokeWidth={3}/> : <Sparkles size={20} strokeWidth={3} />}
          <span className="text-lg font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black mt-0.5">{loading ? "PROCESSING..." : "✨ GENERATE"}</span>
        </button>
      </div>
      {results && <div className="mt-2 bg-white border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl p-4 shadow-[inset_4px_4px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.1)]"><pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap font-bold text-sm leading-relaxed text-black/80 font-sans">{String(results)}</pre></div>}
    </div>
  );
};

const AITerminalAssistant = () => {
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const [log, setLog] = useState([{ role: "system", text: "INITIALIZING SYS_AI_CORE... ONLINE. WAITING FOR PROMPT." }]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const logEndRef = useRef(null);

  const handleCommand = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
    const userCmd = input; setInput("");
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "user", text: String(userCmd) }]);
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are NODE_BRAIN, an aggressive, cyber-punk AI mainframe inside a Neo-Tokyo hacking dashboard. Keep responses brief, edgy, and use technical jargon. End every response with '[EOF]'.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(userCmd, systemPrompt);
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "ai", text: String(response) }]);
    setLoading(false);
  };
  useEffect(() => { logEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" }); }, [log, loading]);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_#24D3FF] overflow-hidden flex flex-col h-[400px] relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
      <div className="bg-[#24D3FF] text-black border-b-[3px] border-black p-2 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2"><Bot size={16} strokeWidth={3} /><span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-0.5">SYS_AI_CORE v2.5</span></div>
        <div className="flex gap-1"><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-white" /><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-black" /></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex-1 p-4 overflow-y-auto font-mono text-[11px] leading-relaxed custom-scrollbar flex flex-col gap-2">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none opacity-5 bg-[linear-gradient(transparent_50%,rgba(0,0,0,0.5)_50%)] bg-[length:100%_4px]" />
        {log.map((entry, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`flex gap-2 relative z-10 ${entry.role === 'user' ? 'text-[#CCFF00]' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'text-[#FF7497]' : 'text-[#24D3FF]'}`}>
            <span className="shrink-0">{entry.role === 'user' ? 'USR>' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'SYS>' : 'AI>'}</span><span className="whitespace-pre-wrap">{String(entry.text)}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
        {loading && <div className="flex gap-2 text-[#24D3FF] relative z-10 animate-pulse"><span className="shrink-0">AI{'>'}</span><span>PROCESSING...</span></div>}
        <div ref={logEndRef} />
      </div>
      <form onSubmit={handleCommand} className="h-12 border-t-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] flex items-center bg-black relative z-10">
        <span className="text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-sm pl-4 pr-2">C:\&gt;</span>
        <input type="text" value={input} onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter command query..." className="flex-1 h-full bg-transparent text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-[11px] uppercase tracking-widest outline-none placeholder:text-[#CCFF00]/30" />
        <button type="submit" disabled={loading} className="h-full px-4 border-l-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#24D3FF] text-black hover:bg-white transition-colors flex items-center justify-center disabled:opacity-50">✨ <Send size={14} className="ml-1" strokeWidth={3}/></button>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
};

const AdvancedRotaryDial = ({ label, targetVal, currentVal, onChange }) => {
  const dialRef = useRef(null);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [startY, setStartY] = useState(0);

  const handlePointerDown = (e) => { setIsDragging(true); setStartY(e.clientY); };
  useEffect(() => {
    const handlePointerMove = (e) => {
      if (isDragging) {
        const delta = startY - e.clientY;
        let newVal = currentVal + delta;
        if (newVal > 100) newVal = 100;
        if (newVal < 0) newVal = 0;
        onChange(newVal);
        setStartY(e.clientY);
      }
    };
    const handlePointerUp = () => setIsDragging(false);
    if (isDragging) { window.addEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove); window.addEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp); }
    return () => { window.removeEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove); window.removeEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp); };
  }, [isDragging, startY, currentVal, onChange]);

  const rotation = (currentVal / 100) * 270 - 135; 
  return (
    <div className="relative p-4 border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full min-h-[160px] select-none">
      <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black bg-[#CCFF00] px-2 border-[2px] border-black absolute top-2 left-2 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black]">{label}</span>
      <div ref={dialRef} onPointerDown={handlePointerDown} className="w-24 h-24 mt-4 rounded-full border-[6px] border-black bg-gray-200 shadow-[inset_0px_0px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5),4px_4px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center justify-center cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors" style={{ transform: `rotate(${rotation}deg)` }}>
        <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full border-[2px] border-dashed border-black/30" />
        <div className="absolute top-2 w-3 h-3 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full border-[2px] border-black shadow-[0_0_5px_#FF7497]" />
      </div>
      <div className="w-full flex justify-between mt-4 px-2 text-[10px] font-black font-mono">
        <span className="opacity-50">MIN</span>
        <span className={`${Math.abs(currentVal - targetVal) < 2 ? 'text-[#24D3FF] scale-125' : 'text-black'} transition-all`}>{Math.round(currentVal)}</span>
        <span className="opacity-50">MAX</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// --- PACK: RUBE GOLDBERG PUZZLE ---
const RubeGoldbergPuzzle = () => {
  const [switches, setSwitches] = useState([false, true, false]);
  const targetSwitches = [true, false, true];
  const isPowerRouted = switches.every((v, i) => v === targetSwitches[i]);
  const [pressure, setPressure] = useState(0);
  const isPressureMaxed = pressure >= 100;
  const [dialVal, setDialVal] = useState(0);
  const targetDial = 88;
  const isDialTuned = Math.abs(dialVal - targetDial) < 2; 
  const isCoreUnlocked = isPowerRouted && isPressureMaxed && isDialTuned;
  const [launched, setLaunched] = useState(false);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-8 border-[6px] border-black rounded-[32px] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[16px_16px_0px_0px_#CCFF00] overflow-hidden flex flex-col p-6 relative min-h-[500px]">
      <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 w-32 h-full bg-[repeating-linear-gradient(45deg,transparent,transparent_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_20px)] pointer-events-none" />
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center border-b-[4px] border-[#24D3FF] pb-4 mb-6 relative z-10">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-black border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] rounded-full flex items-center justify-center"><Cpu size={24} className="text-[#CCFF00]" /></div>
          <div><h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-widest text-white leading-none">THE CORE</h3><p className="text-[10px] font-mono text-[#24D3FF] mt-1">SEQ_UNLOCK_REQUIRED</p></div>
        </div>
        <div className={`px-4 py-2 border-[3px] border-black font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-sm ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'bg-[#CCFF00] text-black shadow-[0_0_15px_#CCFF00]' : 'bg-black text-[#FF7497]'}`}>
          {isCoreUnlocked ? 'UNLOCKED' : 'LOCKED'}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-6 relative z-10 flex-1">
        <div className="flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0 hidden md:block" />
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-white px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">1. ROUTE POWER</span>
          <div className="flex justify-around mt-2">
            {[0, 1, 2].map((i) => (
              <button key={i} onClick={() => setSwitches(prev => { const n = [...prev]; n[i] = !n[i]; return n; })} className="w-12 h-20 bg-gray-200 border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg relative shadow-[inset_0_4px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.2)]">
                <div className={`absolute left-0 right-0 h-10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-md transition-all duration-200 ${switches[i] ? 'top-0 bg-[#CCFF00]' : 'bottom-0 bg-[#FF7497]'}`} />
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black mt-auto ${isPowerRouted ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-500'}`}>{isPowerRouted ? 'ROUTED' : 'MISMATCH'}</div>
        </div>
        <div className={`flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 transition-opacity relative ${!isPowerRouted ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0 hidden md:block" /> 
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-[#24D3FF] px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">2. MAX PRESSURE</span>
          <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center">
             <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={pressure} onChange={(e) => setPressure(parseInt(e.target.value))} className="w-full h-8 bg-black/10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none cursor-pointer" style={{background: `linear-gradient(to right, #FF7497 ${pressure}%, transparent ${pressure}%)`}} />
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black mt-auto ${isPressureMaxed ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-black'}`}>{pressure}%</div>
        </div>
        <div className={`flex-1 transition-opacity ${!isPressureMaxed ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
           <AdvancedRotaryDial label="3. TUNE TO 88" targetVal={targetDial} currentVal={dialVal} onChange={setDialVal} />
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className={`mt-8 pt-8 border-t-[4px] border-dashed border-[#24D3FF]/30 flex flex-col items-center justify-center relative transition-all ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'scale-100 opacity-100' : 'scale-95 opacity-50 pointer-events-none'}`}>
        {launched && (
           <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#CCFF00] z-20 flex items-center justify-center animate-pulse rounded-2xl border-[6px] border-black">
             <h2 className="text-4xl font-[1000] text-black tracking-tighter uppercase">CORE INITIATED</h2>
           </div>
        )}
        <button onClick={() => setLaunched(true)} className={`w-32 h-32 rounded-full border-[8px] border-black flex items-center justify-center shadow-[0_15px_0_0_black,0_0_30px_#FF7497] transition-all hover:translate-y-2 hover:shadow-[0_10px_0_0_black,0_0_40px_#FF7497] active:translate-y-4 active:shadow-[0_0px_0_0_black] relative group bg-[#FF7497]`}>
          <div className="absolute inset-0 rounded-full bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_left,rgba(255,255,255,0.4),transparent_60%)] pointer-events-none" />
          <Power size={48} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black relative z-10 group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform" />
        </button>
        <span className="text-white font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-6 text-sm">4. INITIATE</span>

const VariantLabel = ({ type }) => {
  let styles = "bg-[#FFE357] text-black";
  if (type === "Tokyo-Pop") styles = "bg-[#B28DFF] text-black";
  if (type === "Neo-Tokyo") styles = "bg-white text-black border-[3px] border-black shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_#24D3FF]";
  return (
    <div className={`absolute -top-3 -right-3 px-3 py-1 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest z-20 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center gap-1 ${styles}`}>
      {type === "Neo-Tokyo" && <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full mr-1 animate-pulse" />}{type}
    </div>
  );
};

// --- GEMINI API INTEGRATION ---
const callGeminiAPI = async (prompt, systemInstruction = null) => {
  const apiKey = ""; 
  const url = `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash-preview-09-2025:generateContent?key=${apiKey}`;
  const payload = { contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }] };
  if (systemInstruction) payload.systemInstruction = { parts: [{ text: systemInstruction }] };
  let retries = 5, delay = 1000;
  while (retries > 0) {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(url, { method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" }, body: JSON.stringify(payload) });
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
      const result = await response.json();
      const text = result?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
      return text ? String(text) : "Error: No text generated.";
    } catch (error) {
      retries -= 1;
      if (retries === 0) return `[ERR_FATAL] API call failed: ${error.message}`;
      await new Promise(res => setTimeout(res, delay));
      delay *= 2;
    }
  }
};

const AITitleGenerator = () => {
  const [concept, setConcept] = useState("");
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [results, setResults] = useState("");

  const handleGenerate = async () => {
    if (!concept) return;
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are a hyper-creative YouTube strategist. The user gives you a video concept. Generate 3 highly engaging, clickable YouTube video titles and a 1-sentence hook for each. Format the output cleanly with bullet points. DO NOT use markdown headers, just plain text with numbers and dashes.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(`Video concept: ${concept}`, systemPrompt);
    setResults(String(response));
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[4px] border-black rounded-2xl bg-[#FFE357] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-6 flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Standard" />
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 border-b-[4px] border-black pb-4">
        <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-white border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black]"><Sparkles size={24} strokeWidth={3} className="text-[#FF7497]" /></div>
        <div><h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black leading-none">AI Idea Studio</h3><p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black/60 mt-1">Powered by Gemini API</p></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-4">
        <input type="text" value={concept} onChange={(e) => setConcept(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter rough video concept..." className="flex-1 h-14 border-[3px] border-black rounded-xl pl-4 pr-4 font-black uppercase text-sm outline-none focus:bg-white transition-colors shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] bg-[#f3f4f6]" />
        <button onClick={handleGenerate} disabled={loading || !concept} className="h-14 px-8 bg-[#CCFF00] border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl shadow-[4px_4px_0px_0px_black] hover:-translate-y-1 hover:shadow-[4px_6px_0px_0px_black] active:translate-y-1 active:shadow-none transition-all flex items-center justify-center gap-2 disabled:opacity-50">
          {loading ? <Loader2 size={20} className="animate-spin" strokeWidth={3}/> : <Sparkles size={20} strokeWidth={3} />}
          <span className="text-lg font-[900] uppercase tracking-tighter text-black mt-0.5">{loading ? "PROCESSING..." : "✨ GENERATE"}</span>
        </button>
      </div>
      {results && <div className="mt-2 bg-white border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl p-4 shadow-[inset_4px_4px_0px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.1)]"><pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap font-bold text-sm leading-relaxed text-black/80 font-sans">{String(results)}</pre></div>}
    </div>
  );
};

const AITerminalAssistant = () => {
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const [log, setLog] = useState([{ role: "system", text: "INITIALIZING SYS_AI_CORE... ONLINE. WAITING FOR PROMPT." }]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const logEndRef = useRef(null);

  const handleCommand = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
    const userCmd = input; setInput("");
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "user", text: String(userCmd) }]);
    setLoading(true);
    const systemPrompt = "You are NODE_BRAIN, an aggressive, cyber-punk AI mainframe inside a Neo-Tokyo hacking dashboard. Keep responses brief, edgy, and use technical jargon. End every response with '[EOF]'.";
    const response = await callGeminiAPI(userCmd, systemPrompt);
    setLog(prev => [...prev, { role: "ai", text: String(response) }]);
    setLoading(false);
  };
  useEffect(() => { logEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" }); }, [log, loading]);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_#24D3FF] overflow-hidden flex flex-col h-[400px] relative">
      <VariantLabel type="Tokyo-Pop" />
      <div className="bg-[#24D3FF] text-black border-b-[3px] border-black p-2 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2"><Bot size={16} strokeWidth={3} /><span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-0.5">SYS_AI_CORE v2.5</span></div>
        <div className="flex gap-1"><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-white" /><div className="w-3 h-3 border-[2px] border-black bg-black" /></div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex-1 p-4 overflow-y-auto font-mono text-[11px] leading-relaxed custom-scrollbar flex flex-col gap-2">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none opacity-5 bg-[linear-gradient(transparent_50%,rgba(0,0,0,0.5)_50%)] bg-[length:100%_4px]" />
        {log.map((entry, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`flex gap-2 relative z-10 ${entry.role === 'user' ? 'text-[#CCFF00]' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'text-[#FF7497]' : 'text-[#24D3FF]'}`}>
            <span className="shrink-0">{entry.role === 'user' ? 'USR>' : entry.role === 'system' ? 'SYS>' : 'AI>'}</span><span className="whitespace-pre-wrap">{String(entry.text)}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
        {loading && <div className="flex gap-2 text-[#24D3FF] relative z-10 animate-pulse"><span className="shrink-0">AI{'>'}</span><span>PROCESSING...</span></div>}
        <div ref={logEndRef} />
      </div>
      <form onSubmit={handleCommand} className="h-12 border-t-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] flex items-center bg-black relative z-10">
        <span className="text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-sm pl-4 pr-2">C:\&gt;</span>
        <input type="text" value={input} onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)} placeholder="Enter command query..." className="flex-1 h-full bg-transparent text-[#CCFF00] font-mono text-[11px] uppercase tracking-widest outline-none placeholder:text-[#CCFF00]/30" />
        <button type="submit" disabled={loading} className="h-full px-4 border-l-[2px] border-[#24D3FF] bg-[#24D3FF] text-black hover:bg-white transition-colors flex items-center justify-center disabled:opacity-50">✨ <Send size={14} className="ml-1" strokeWidth={3}/></button>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
};

const AdvancedRotaryDial = ({ label, targetVal, currentVal, onChange }) => {
  const dialRef = useRef(null);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [startY, setStartY] = useState(0);

  const handlePointerDown = (e) => { setIsDragging(true); setStartY(e.clientY); };
  useEffect(() => {
    const handlePointerMove = (e) => {
      if (isDragging) {
        const delta = startY - e.clientY;
        let newVal = currentVal + delta;
        if (newVal > 100) newVal = 100;
        if (newVal < 0) newVal = 0;
        onChange(newVal);
        setStartY(e.clientY);
      }
    };
    const handlePointerUp = () => setIsDragging(false);
    if (isDragging) { window.addEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove); window.addEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp); }
    return () => { window.removeEventListener('pointermove', handlePointerMove); window.removeEventListener('pointerup', handlePointerUp); };
  }, [isDragging, startY, currentVal, onChange]);

  const rotation = (currentVal / 100) * 270 - 135; 
  return (
    <div className="relative p-4 border-[4px] border-black rounded-xl bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full min-h-[160px] select-none">
      <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-black bg-[#CCFF00] px-2 border-[2px] border-black absolute top-2 left-2 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black]">{label}</span>
      <div ref={dialRef} onPointerDown={handlePointerDown} className="w-24 h-24 mt-4 rounded-full border-[6px] border-black bg-gray-200 shadow-[inset_0px_0px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5),4px_4px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center justify-center cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing hover:bg-gray-100 transition-colors" style={{ transform: `rotate(${rotation}deg)` }}>
        <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full border-[2px] border-dashed border-black/30" />
        <div className="absolute top-2 w-3 h-3 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full border-[2px] border-black shadow-[0_0_5px_#FF7497]" />
      </div>
      <div className="w-full flex justify-between mt-4 px-2 text-[10px] font-black font-mono">
        <span className="opacity-50">MIN</span>
        <span className={`${Math.abs(currentVal - targetVal) < 2 ? 'text-[#24D3FF] scale-125' : 'text-black'} transition-all`}>{Math.round(currentVal)}</span>
        <span className="opacity-50">MAX</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const RubeGoldbergPuzzle = () => {
  const [switches, setSwitches] = useState([false, true, false]);
  const targetSwitches = [true, false, true];
  const isPowerRouted = switches.every((v, i) => v === targetSwitches[i]);
  const [pressure, setPressure] = useState(0);
  const isPressureMaxed = pressure >= 100;
  const [dialVal, setDialVal] = useState(0);
  const targetDial = 88;
  const isDialTuned = Math.abs(dialVal - targetDial) < 2; 
  const isCoreUnlocked = isPowerRouted && isPressureMaxed && isDialTuned;
  const [launched, setLaunched] = useState(false);

  return (
    <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-8 border-[6px] border-black rounded-[32px] bg-[#1A1A24] shadow-[16px_16px_0px_0px_#CCFF00] overflow-hidden flex flex-col p-6 relative min-h-[500px]">
      <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 w-32 h-full bg-[repeating-linear-gradient(45deg,transparent,transparent_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_10px,rgba(255,255,255,0.05)_20px)] pointer-events-none" />
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center border-b-[4px] border-[#24D3FF] pb-4 mb-6 relative z-10">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-black border-[3px] border-[#24D3FF] rounded-full flex items-center justify-center"><Cpu size={24} className="text-[#CCFF00]" /></div>
          <div><h3 className="text-2xl font-[900] uppercase tracking-widest text-white leading-none">THE CORE</h3><p className="text-[10px] font-mono text-[#24D3FF] mt-1">SEQ_UNLOCK_REQUIRED</p></div>
        </div>
        <div className={`px-4 py-2 border-[3px] border-black font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-sm ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'bg-[#CCFF00] text-black shadow-[0_0_15px_#CCFF00]' : 'bg-black text-[#FF7497]'}`}>
          {isCoreUnlocked ? 'UNLOCKED' : 'LOCKED'}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-6 relative z-10 flex-1">
        <div className="flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 relative">
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0 hidden md:block" />
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-white px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">1. ROUTE POWER</span>
          <div className="flex justify-around mt-2">
            {[0, 1, 2].map((i) => (
              <button key={i} onClick={() => setSwitches(prev => { const n = [...prev]; n[i] = !n[i]; return n; })} className="w-12 h-20 bg-gray-200 border-[3px] border-black rounded-lg relative shadow-[inset_0_4px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.2)]">
                <div className={`absolute left-0 right-0 h-10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-md transition-all duration-200 ${switches[i] ? 'top-0 bg-[#CCFF00]' : 'bottom-0 bg-[#FF7497]'}`} />
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black mt-auto ${isPowerRouted ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-500'}`}>{isPowerRouted ? 'ROUTED' : 'MISMATCH'}</div>
        </div>
        <div className={`flex-1 border-[4px] border-black bg-white shadow-[8px_8px_0px_0px_black] p-4 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4 transition-opacity relative ${!isPowerRouted ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
          <div className="absolute -right-3 top-1/2 w-6 h-2 bg-black z-0 hidden md:block" /> 
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase bg-black text-[#24D3FF] px-2 w-max border-[2px] border-black">2. MAX PRESSURE</span>
          <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center">
             <input type="range" min="0" max="100" value={pressure} onChange={(e) => setPressure(parseInt(e.target.value))} className="w-full h-8 bg-black/10 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full appearance-none cursor-pointer" style={{background: `linear-gradient(to right, #FF7497 ${pressure}%, transparent ${pressure}%)`}} />
          </div>
          <div className={`text-center font-mono text-[10px] font-black mt-auto ${isPressureMaxed ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-black'}`}>{pressure}%</div>
        </div>
        <div className={`flex-1 transition-opacity ${!isPressureMaxed ? 'opacity-40 pointer-events-none' : ''}`}>
           <AdvancedRotaryDial label="3. TUNE TO 88" targetVal={targetDial} currentVal={dialVal} onChange={setDialVal} />
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className={`mt-8 pt-8 border-t-[4px] border-dashed border-[#24D3FF]/30 flex flex-col items-center justify-center relative transition-all ${isCoreUnlocked ? 'scale-100 opacity-100' : 'scale-95 opacity-50 pointer-events-none'}`}>
        {launched && (
           <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[#CCFF00] z-20 flex items-center justify-center animate-pulse rounded-2xl border-[6px] border-black">
             <h2 className="text-4xl font-[1000] text-black tracking-tighter uppercase">CORE INITIATED</h2>
           </div>
        )}
        <button onClick={() => setLaunched(true)} className={`w-32 h-32 rounded-full border-[8px] border-black flex items-center justify-center shadow-[0_15px_0_0_black,0_0_30px_#FF7497] transition-all hover:translate-y-2 hover:shadow-[0_10px_0_0_black,0_0_40px_#FF7497] active:translate-y-4 active:shadow-[0_0px_0_0_black] relative group bg-[#FF7497]`}>
          <div className="absolute inset-0 rounded-full bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_left,rgba(255,255,255,0.4),transparent_60%)] pointer-events-none" />
          <Power size={48} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black relative z-10 group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform" />
        </button>
        <span className="text-white font-black uppercase tracking-widest mt-6 text-sm">4. INITIATE</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const VariantLabel = ({ type }) => {
  let styles = "bg-[#FFE357] text-black";
  if (type === "Tokyo-Pop") styles = "bg-[#B28DFF] text-black";
  if (type === "Neo-Tokyo") styles = "bg-white text-black border-[3px] border-black shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_#24D3FF]";
  return (
    <div className={`absolute -top-3 -right-3 px-3 py-1 border-[3px] border-black rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest z-20 shadow-[2px_2px_0px_0px_black] flex items-center gap-1 ${styles}`}>
      {type === "Neo-Tokyo" && <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-[#FF7497] rounded-full mr-1 animate-pulse" />}{type}
    </div>
  );
};

    {open ? <Minimize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" /> : <Maximize2 size={size * 0.6} strokeWidth={3} className="text-black" />}
  </div>
);

    return (

        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};
